Foreign Military Attaches Investigate Japan in Large Numbers 96

According to the Osaka Mainichi Newspaper of July 20th, recently, the number of foreign military attaches coming to Japan under the guise of tourism has suddenly increased. According to investigations by the military police authorities, from January to June of this year, the number of people coming to Japan in this six-month period totaled 152 from Country A, 62 from Country B, and 18 from other countries. Calculated by month, there were 19 in January, 20 in February, 26 in March, 45 in April, 86 in May, and 36 in June. Among them, 102 were military attaches from Country A stationed in ○○○, 15 were military attaches from the Country B ○○○ fleet, 23 were military attaches from Country B stationed in ○○, and 92 were from other countries. They mostly inspect important cities and, under the pretext of inspecting battle sites, thoroughly investigate the Najin Port, the Gilhoe Line, the Korean Inland Railway, and airfields along the Yalu River from Sinuiju in Korea, and Manchuria, and North China. The large number of military attaches visiting Japan is noteworthy, and is likely related to the Manchurian problem. Since the September 18th Incident, many have been sent to inspect the military situation and national conditions of our country (Japan). The military police are paying close attention to their actions because the majority are engaged in military reconnaissance.

Handover of the Palace Museum Awaits 97

Secretary-General Xu Hongbao Arrives at the Academy to Reorganize the Xi'an Branch of Antiquities, Pending Discussion by the Next Council Meeting, Special Dispatch from Peiping: Ma Heng, the newly appointed acting director of the Palace Museum, is currently in Shanghai negotiating various matters and is temporarily unable to return to Peiping to assume his duties. However, in order to reorganize the museum's affairs, Ma first telegraphed Xu Hongbao, a council member of the museum in Peiping, to be the secretary-general. Xu arrived at the museum at 10 a.m. on the 28th to take up his duties and convened a meeting of the staff to give instructions. On the 29th, Xu and senior staff discussed various important issues. The situation is recorded as follows:

Encouraging Staff 98

Xu Hongbao arrived at the museum by car at 10 a.m. on the 28th. After a brief rest, he convened a meeting of all staff to give instructions, stating briefly that he had received a telegram from Director Ma instructing him to come to the museum to work. "Most of you are acquaintances. With familiar faces and skilled hands, everything will naturally

Page 15

be easier. The work of each department will continue as usual. I hope you will all help a lot. If you have any suggestions, I will convey them to Director Ma after he returns to Peiping so that they can be considered for adoption."

Handover Procedures 99

Today (the 29th) at 10 a.m., Xu Hongbao invited Secretary Wu Ying for a conversation in the Secretary-General's office to discuss handover procedures. The Palace Museum has too many treasures. Due to the tense situation in the past, apart from the 14,000 crates of antiquities transported south, the number of antiquities remaining in Peiping is difficult to count. Although there is an inventory, it is quite difficult to verify. The starting point for the handover in the future, whether it will be one palace or several palaces simultaneously, and the supervisory personnel, handover personnel, etc., all need to be considered in advance. Most of the antiquities from the east and west routes have been transported away, making handover easier. The central route has a large number of antiquities, making it difficult to hand over. After three hours of confidential discussion, the basic principles of the handover were decided. However, detailed and specific measures still need to be referred to the acting director, Ma Heng.

Branch System 100

Regarding the establishment of branch museums of the Palace Museum, Zhang Ji, a member of the Western Capital Preparatory Committee, advocated that all the documents and books from the museum's Literature and Documents Library should be moved to Xi'an. However, quite a few central committee members opposed this proposal. The branch museum system will be discussed at the next council meeting, which is expected to be held in Nanjing in September. Council members Sun Ke, Zhu Jiahua, Gu Mengyu, Ju Zheng, Wu Dingchang, Ye Gongchuo, Liu Shouzhong, Qian Yongming, Chu Minyi, Shi Liangcai, Zhou Zuomin, Ye Chucang, and Zhang Jia'ao are expected to attend. After the council decides on a plan, it will be submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. Branch museums will be established in Nanjing, Shanghai, and Xi'an. The antiquities displayed in the branch museums will be limited to duplicate items from the Palace Museum that have been reviewed by experts and deemed suitable for display in different locations. However, this must wait until a detailed catalog is published and reviewed before they can be moved. As for the items allocated by the Palace Museum Council to the branch museums, a detailed catalog should be compiled and published under the names of the council and the branch museums. However, the establishment of the Xi'an branch museum is extremely difficult. The government has no large funds allocated for construction costs, and it is not easy for the Xi'an administrative agencies and academia to raise funds for construction. Even if construction is possible, the architectural form and plan must first be deemed appropriate by the Palace Museum Council before construction can begin. Only after the buildings are completed can the antiquities be moved. The problem of the premises for the Shanghai and Nanjing branch museums is also not easy to solve. (July 29th, Jin)

He Jian's Deployment to Suppress Bandits in Jiangxi 101

West Route Commander-in-Chief Headquarters to Move to Pingxiang, Li Jue Acting as Security Commander and Deputy Commander of the Entire Province, He Jian's Proclamation Urges the People in Bandit Areas to Quickly Turn Over a New Leaf, Dispatch from Changsha: The West Route Commander-in-Chief Headquarters of the Jiangxi, Guangdong, Fujian, Hunan, and Hubei Bandit Suppression Army is now deployed and ready to depart, and will soon move to Pingxiang in Jiangxi to command everything. Commander-in-Chief He Jian believes that with the large army penetrating deep into Jiangxi, the security of Hunan Province is extremely important. Therefore, he submitted a request to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and Minister He for approval to have Li Jue, commander of the 19th Division, act as the security commander and deputy commander of the entire province, responsible for maintaining security within Hunan Province. All of the 19th Division and the Li Guojun Brigade of the 62nd Division, the Chen Zixian Brigade of the 63rd Division, the Hunan Provincial Capital Garrison Commander and its subordinate units, all water and land police agencies in Hunan Province related to military affairs, and armored vehicle teams, etc., are under his command and dispatch. Li Jue was ordered to report to the headquarters immediately to take over and assume responsibility. However, He's plan to suppress bandits focuses on winning back the people. Young men and women who have been misled by bandits or local people who have been coerced into working for the bandits will be allowed to surrender and turn over a new leaf, without being held accountable for the past, and will be guaranteed safety, as a radical solution. Therefore, before departing, he issued a proclamation ordering all units to post it in the bandit areas. At the same time, a propaganda team was organized, with Li Shaoling, the head of the Party Affairs Section of the Party and Government Department of the headquarters, concurrently serving as the team leader, to depart with the army immediately for propaganda, in order to achieve practical results. The following is an excerpt from He's proclamation: [Now that the army is suppressing bandits to save the people, all our troops will strictly abide by discipline, without any disturbances, get along with the people, and maintain a peaceful attitude of fair buying and selling. You can all live and work in peace, without having to move or relocate, and without causing unnecessary alarm. If any young men and women have been misled by bandits or local people have been coerced into working for the bandits, this commander-in-chief will be lenient. As long as you realize your mistakes and turn back, quickly surrender and turn over a new leaf, and we will never hold you accountable for your past crimes. If you can expose the secrets of the bandits or surrender with weapons, you will be rewarded heavily. This is hereby announced, hoping that you will persuade each other to leave the bandit party and return in good faith. If there are any who are stubborn and resist to the end, when the army arrives, they will be severely punished without leniency. Now, the important conditions are listed below for the public to understand: (1) Amnesty for those who surrender and turn over a new leaf for their past crimes, and private retaliation is prohibited. (2) Guarantee the lives of those who surrender and turn over a new leaf, and all legal rights and obligations. (3) Protect the property of local residents, and distribute the grain seized from the bandits to the residents. (4) Provide relief grain to returning residents or allocate land for them to cultivate. (5) All old debts and land taxes before the 21st year of the Republic in the bandit areas will be waived. (6) Heavy rewards will be given to those who surrender with weapons or report bandit information. (7) Those who surrender in groups with weapons will have their leaders promoted, and those who follow will be heavily rewarded. (8) Those who are injured in battle or who are sick and cannot get medical treatment will be sent to the hospital for treatment. (9) The army will never [leave] until the scattered bandits are eliminated and the area is at peace. (10) Organizing a Communist eradication volunteer team is a good way to defend against the trampling of the Communist bandits, and it is not to conscript you or raise funds. (11) Strict household registration checks in various places are to prevent the Communist bandits from secretly organizing and the bandits from staying behind. (12) Those who pretend to surrender but secretly work for the bandits will be killed. (13) Those who collude with the army to spy on military intelligence will be killed. (14) Those who communicate with the bandits or smuggle goods to the bandit areas will be killed. (15) Those who damage power lines, roads, and military works will be killed. The top eight items give you great benefits, and the top seven items are necessary measures to protect the locality. This commander-in-chief loves the people like his own children, and sincerely explains, hoping that you will all advise your fathers and sons, brothers, and neighbors, and turn away from your former mistakes and become good people together. This commander-in-chief has great expectations. ] (July 27th)

Current Financial Situation in Hubei Province 102

Sharp Decline in Revenue, Only 30% of Land Tax Collected, Living on Borrowed Money, Construction and Education Stalled, Dispatch from Wuchang: Due to recent natural disasters and man-made calamities in Hubei Province, rural areas have gone bankrupt, resulting in a significant impact on the province's treasury revenue. According to investigations, the province's treasury revenue was originally mainly derived from land tax, with an annual quota of approximately 2 million yuan. In the previous two years, the average collection was only 70%, or 1.2 million yuan per year. In the 21st year of the Republic, due to the increasingly depressed rural economy, land tax revenue was reduced to just over 600,000 yuan, which is only 30% of the original quota. According to accurate statistics, the actual monthly revenue in the 21st year of the Republic is listed as follows:

July of the 21st year of the Republic: 20,440 yuan; August: 38,535 yuan; September: 15,203 yuan; October: 124,568 yuan; November: 93,278 yuan; December: 114,675 yuan; January of the 22nd year of the Republic: 20,958 yuan; February: 14,233 yuan; March: 54,168 yuan; April: 32,004 yuan; May: 67,309 yuan; June: 49,354 yuan; Total: 644,725 yuan.

Also, since the implementation of the abolition of likin (internal tariffs) in the province, tax revenue has also decreased. The income and expenditure are far from sufficient, and the province has resorted to borrowing money to make ends meet. According to investigations, in the past year, from April of the 21st year to March of this year, a total of over 6,263,000 yuan has been borrowed from various banks. From June of the 21st year to April of this year (11 months), a total of over 349,000 yuan has been collected from borrowed house rents. The total is over 6,613,500 yuan. The province's treasury's income and expenditure for the past month, totaling over 3 million yuan, is recorded below to show the situation of government expenditure allocation: (A) Income: Land tax 49,354.890, deed tax 20,048.88, brokerage tax 11,022.310, salt tax 600, slaughter tax 8,154.910, business tax 246,040.032, public property income 19,745.170, business income 370.300, regular and surcharge taxes 18,717.240, administrative income 6,458.249, judicial income 24.560, income from securities 11,810.160, miscellaneous income 433.650, budget surplus 11,819.330, public loan income 292,460.630, subsidy 615,039.230, borrowed funds 69,968.120, lump-sum payment 100,000, Hankou city income 1,953,235.540, previous month's inventory 90,667.630, total income 3,532,321.8211 yuan.

(B) Expenditure: Land tax 64,500, repayment of borrowed funds 139,328.750, advances 2,770.000, temporary notes 31,344.910, party affairs expenses 25,557.840, administrative expenses 73,170.127, reserve fund 105,345.800, public security expenses 235,884.660, financial expenses 64,905.654, education and cultural expenses 146,975.780, agriculture and mining 3,647.150, industry and commerce 3,686.880, construction expenses 35,287.390, health expenses 1,726.270, judicial expenses 59,672.090, official business expenses 260,611.240, Hankou expenditure 1,953,235.920, interest 134,894.920, subsidies 630.000, public debt expenditure 86,500.000, surplus 167,082.730, total expenditure 3,532,321.831 yuan.

The surplus for the month is 167,082 yuan, but after deducting the 98,085 yuan for June government expenses, the actual surplus is 68,995 yuan. Also, the separate listing of income and expenditure for Hankou is a transfer account of income and expenditure from October 11th of the 21st year to April 30th of the 22nd year. From the above table, it can be seen that the fiscal revenue of Hubei Province relies heavily on borrowing, while the expenditure on industry, commerce, education, culture, agriculture, mining, and health is very low. (17th)

The Yellow River Has Entered a Dangerous Situation 103

| Han Orders County Magistrates Along the River to Move to the Dikes for Defense |

Dispatch from Jinan: The water level of the Yellow River in Shandong Province has been increasing recently, gradually presenting a serious situation. All the people of Shandong are worried about this. The provincial government recently received a telegram from the Shaanxi provincial government stating that the Yellow River had breached its banks in Yongji County, Shanxi Province, and the floodwaters were rushing south, affecting Pingmin County in Shaanxi Province, informing the downstream provinces to take strict precautions to avoid being flooded. Compared with the annual flooding situation of the Yellow River in Shandong Province, the longest continuous rise in water level is three days. This year, the water level has been rising since July 21st, and it has already been seven days (28th). The water level in each section is still rising continuously. Moreover, according to the Yellow River's custom, the water level will inevitably rise sharply around the Beginning of Autumn, which is regarded as the flood season and the most dangerous period for river works. Now, before the arrival of the great flood season, the water level at Zhongluokou today (28th) actually reached 30.05 meters, only 0.05 meters lower than the highest water level last year. Furthermore, according to the speculation of experienced experts, the water level in the upper reaches is still high, and it is unknown whether it will create a new water level record in the future. Under this current situation, the lives and property of millions of people along the river depend on the dikes. Therefore, Provincial Chairman Han Fuju and Director of the River Affairs Bureau Zhang Lianjia are extremely anxious about this, and they have jointly discussed protection measures. Han Fuju also telegraphed today to the magistrates of Licheng, Changqing, Qihhe, Jiyang, Qidong, Qingcheng, Feicheng, Dongping, Pingyin, Juancheng, Huimin, Binzhou, Putai, Lijin, Zhanhua, and Qiu counties, a total of 22 counties along the river, ordering them to move to the dikes for defense for seven days starting from today, in order to jointly supervise the soldiers and laborers to assist in the defense with the river workers, and to report the dates of arrival and departure at work at any time for examination, in order to emphasize the importance of the dikes.

The River Affairs Bureau received a report from Dongzhuang in the upper reaches today that the water level had slightly decreased, but the water level was still at 58.8 meters. At Guanzhuang, it rose 1.2 inches, and the water level was 35.91 meters, which is the highest recorded water level in previous years. At Scorpion Bay in the lower reaches, it rose another 7 centimeters, and the water level was 18.27 meters. The situation of the entire river has entered a dangerous state. In order to prevent any eventuality, it is planned to raise the dikes along the river, which will be three feet higher than last year. Even if the river water rises another foot this year, the dike will still be two feet higher than the water surface. If no other changes occur, the river works can be guaranteed to be safe. In order to understand the water level and plan the dikes, Director Zhang Lianjia went to Luokou this morning at 8 o'clock with Zhao Luren, chief of the General Affairs Section of the River Affairs Bureau, Pan Fen, chief of the Engineering Section, and Wen Chenglie, the mayor of Jinan, to inspect and investigate the construction situation. They returned to Jinan around 11 o'clock at noon. (28th)

Gao Yihan of Songjiang Inspects Songjiang 104

Gao Yihan, an inspector of the Control Yuan, arrived in Songjiang today at half past ten by car, accompanied by his secretary Wang. He drove to the commissioner's office, where Commissioner Jin welcomed him and they talked to each other. A banquet was held in the office, inviting Cai Zhongyu of the Chamber of Commerce, Li Jingxian of the Land Production Office, Ni Bingshi of the Storage Association, and Ye Dingchu of the county party department, Shen Jing, the head of the public security bureau, and others to accompany them. After the banquet, a discussion was held, in which Inspector Gao reported that he had come to investigate administration, education, public security, and judicial matters, carrying various survey forms. Secretary Wang was sent to the court and education bureau to fill out the forms separately. Gao paid close attention to the seawall. The attendees stated that the county's seawall had been slightly damaged by the recent hurricane, but it had been repaired. However, it was not a fundamental solution. Repairing the seawall required a huge amount of money, which was beyond the financial capacity of the local government. It was also difficult to obtain funds from the provincial treasury. It was generally agreed that American wheat was used to protect the rural economy. However, if the seawall was not solid, the rural economy could not be developed. As a result, it was proposed that the county should jointly request the allocation of American wheat with Changshu and Baoshan counties to pay for the repair of the seawall. The consensus was that Gao returned to Shanghai by car at 5 p.m. It was said that he had made an appointment to inspect the seawall together at a later date, to facilitate the planning of the project.

Market Strike in Lujiahui, Nanhui 105

Since Captain Zhou of the Salt Police was stationed in Lujiahui, Nanhui, he has indulged his subordinates, and conflicts with the people have occurred repeatedly. Yesterday, a villager brought three catties of salt to Gong Ruixing's clothing store to tailor clothes. It happened to be seen by the salt police, who vented their anger on the sewing worker of the store, causing him to be severely beaten and injured. It was at 1 p.m., just when the villagers were going to the market. Qi Zhaoging, a clerk at the official salt distribution point of Yipinzai, ordered the salt police to fire their guns as a warning, causing panic among the people. Xu Yiqun, a doctor in the town, questioned Zhao Qing for not ordering the salt police to fire their guns, but was attacked by the salt police, who injured the top of his head, causing him to bleed profusely and be detained at the team headquarters. Merchants and people were indignant and went on strike. The head of the ninth district of Hangtou, Shen, learned of the incident and immediately went to Lu to mediate with Police Chief Chen of the Salt Police. Unexpectedly, Police Chief Chen was unreasonable, and the merchants and people felt even more dissatisfied, resulting in a continued strike.

Change of Chief Prosecutor of Suzhou Higher Court 106

Wang Simo, the chief prosecutor of the Jiangsu Higher Court Procuratorate, has been in office for five or six years, and there have long been rumors of a change of personnel. It was not easy to find a suitable candidate to succeed him. It was not until yesterday (31st) that the Ministry's order arrived in Suzhou, transferring Wang to be the president of the Fengyang First Branch of the Anhui Higher Court. The new position of chief prosecutor of the Suzhou Higher Court Procuratorate left vacant will be provisionally filled by Hu Yi-yu, the current president of the Zhenjiang District Court. The vacancy of the president of the Zhenjiang District Court will be filled by Zhong Zhihan, the former director of Jiangning Local Office and the current president of the Hankou District Court.

Lian Tang Water Police in Changshu Arrest Bandits 107

On the night of the 30th, the captain of the 13th squadron of the water police in Liantang Town, 7th District, received a tip-off that two suspected robbers in a certain case had fled to this place. Captain Wang immediately sent plainclothes officers to search. When they arrived at their destination, the two bandits had already heard the news and fled. They were then captured in Pingshi Town and brought back to the team headquarters for questioning. According to their confession, one was Zhao Zhenyou and the other was Xu Jinhua, both from Hefei, Anhui. Their detailed confessions are under investigation and cannot be disclosed. The two, Zhao and Xu, are scheduled to be handed over to the county for questioning on the 31st.

Temple Opera House in Wang City Burned Down 108

The General Manager Temple in Wang City Town, 8th District, was built during the Kangxi period of the Qing Dynasty. There was an opera house, which was spacious, well-decorated, and luxurious. It has been more than 300 years since then. On the night before last (29th) at around 12 o'clock, it suddenly caught fire. By the time the residents went to rescue it, it had become a raging fire. Moreover, because there were no water pumps in the countryside, it was not easy to extinguish. Within two hours, it was completely burned down. There were 26 coffins stored under the building, which were also completely destroyed. The total loss is estimated to be around 5,000 to 6,000 yuan.

Temporary Merchants in Wuxi Collect Business Tax 109

The county government and the business tax bureau of this county have recently received instructions from the Department of Finance that temporary merchants transporting goods are engaged in short-term business and should be collected on a one-time basis according to regulations. Previously, with reference to the Anhui precedent, the method of payment on behalf of the industry was used, and the bureau was ordered to comply. It is now found that the handling of each bureau is not consistent, which is detrimental to tax revenue. A method of collection procedures has been specifically revised and ordered to be followed. The two heads of the county bureau issued a bulletin yesterday after receiving the order, and also sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce, forwarding the letter to various merchants to comply with. Also, the Jiangsu Provincial Federation of Commerce stated that the business tax rate for the 22nd year of the Republic has been repeatedly pleaded for by the chamber of commerce for the merchants, and the provincial department has agreed to continue to handle it according to the current tax rate. Therefore, a letter was specially sent to the county chamber of commerce to assist the tax bureau in collecting taxes, in order to emphasize the importance of the country.

Verdict in the Dajichun Poison Pill Case 110

The Dajichun Pharmacy on Beida Street in this county produced and sold Lin Zexu's opium cessation poison pills. The case was once solved before. On October 16th of last year, Zheng Tingliang, Gu Linxiang, Su Zhongliang, and others went to buy the pills disguised as customers. They immediately called the police on the spot and arrested the manager Wu Nianyun and others, along with the stolen goods. The procuratorate filed a public prosecution, and Judge Lai Sihong repeatedly interrogated them, announcing the end of the debate on the case. Yesterday was the date for the verdict in this case. Judge Lai signed the order to bring Wu Nianyun to the court and announced that Wu Nianyun was guilty of selling opium substitutes and sentenced him to two years of imprisonment and a fine of 1,000 yuan. As for the case of the shop assistants Xu Yizhai, Wu Zhibiao, etc., the main text of the verdict will be posted separately. Wu Nianyun was still returned to custody.

Danyang Detective Team Accused of Torturing Kidnappers 111

Ma Lianfa, alias Chai Amou, a resident of Machang Township, 8th District of the county, was secretly reported to the Public Security Bureau for allegedly kidnapping a Tan surname child from Beigang Village. The bureau immediately sent a detective team to secretly capture Ma. The team leader questioned him and confessed that the Tan surname kidnapping case was related to the killing of Shu Dacheng in Shanghai's Pintang Lane. The General Bureau transferred the case to the county for handling. Later, Ma Lianfa's family came to the county to file a lawsuit against the team for torturing him to force a confession, with bloody clothes as evidence. County Chief Guo considered the case to be serious and immediately sent Section Chief Shen to open a court for investigation. The suspect claimed that the confessions he had made previously were actually the result of illegal torture by the detective team, and that he had been forced to sign them. Based on the confession, Section Chief Shen ordered the medical examiner to examine the scars and ordered him to be detained. The suspect Ma Lianfa has now been taken away by the Shanghai Second District Security Bureau for investigation and handling.

Zhenjiang Telephone Bureau Expansion Plan 112

The new building of the Zhenjiang Telephone Bureau has been designed by the Ministry of Communications and is being put out to tender in Beijing. Construction must begin within the month and be completed within eight months. All lines will be replaced with rubber-sheathed double copper wires. The telephones will use the pre-Nanjing common battery type. No ringing is required during use. When the handset is taken off, the switchboard light will come on. The operator will connect the line, and the other party's phone will ring automatically, which is more convenient than a crank phone. The total number of telephones will be 1,600. If management can be improved at the same time, business can be improved.

Two Bandit Chiefs in Xixiang, Nantong, Sentenced 113

Two bandit chiefs, Tao Dongyan and Yu, in Tongyi Xixiang, were captured by the military police and sent to the county government for trial. The two convicts have confessed to their crimes of robbery and murder over the years. The county magistrate, considering the serious crimes committed by the two convicts, sentenced them to death in accordance with the provincial government's banditry suppression telegram and telegraphed the province for approval.

Establishment of a Specialty Market for Enemy Goods 114

The Party and government agencies in Nantong are now preparing to establish a specialty market for enemy goods at the Quanggongchang in the city, with representatives elected by various industries to preside over it.

Robbery at Tangjiawang Liuchenghang in Yangzhou 115

Ma Wenxun, a resident of Tangjiawang in Yiyi, opened a Liuchenghang in Wang, and had a small amount of savings, which was coveted by bandits. On the night before last, many bandits broke into the house by climbing over the wall. They first twisted Ma's arm and warned him not to make a sound. They went to various places to search and rob, which lasted for an hour before they left with shouts. After checking, they found that a lot of clothes, foreign goods, and ornaments were lost. On the 29th, they rushed to Yangzhou and reported to the county government, requesting the arrest of the thieves and the recovery of the stolen goods.

Bandit Robbery of Grain Boat in Lujiaqiao, Gaoyou 116

Kong Guangcai, a grain merchant, previously loaded a boat of wheat and came to Youyi to sell it at the Hengnan Liuchenghang outside Nanmen, obtaining 400 to 500 yuan. On the morning of the 27th, he took the original boat home. However, when he reached Lujiaqiao in Xihu, he suddenly encountered a [boat] carrying five bandits, each holding a box gun, who ordered him to stop and jumped onto Kong's boat. After searching for a long time, they robbed him of silver coins, clothing, rice, etc., with a loss of about 800 yuan.

District Chief Qin Tortured by Bandits 117

District Chief Qin Shifang, of the 10th District, was kidnapped by bandits in Sanyanghe some time ago. There has been no news of him. According to a released hostage, District Chief Qin is now suffering severe torture in the bandits' den. The bandits used lead wire to wrap around Qin's body and pierce his hand veins, and then used and sharp blades to shave the flesh on his face and body. His body is covered in [wounds], and the sight is unbearable. It is feared that his life is in danger.

Chen, Education Committee Member of Liuhe, Accused of Embezzling Relief Funds 118

Chen Zanong, the Education Committee member and Security Committee member of the Fourth District of this county, was accused by villagers Gu Yongyi and others to the county government for embezzling fifty yuan of relief funds. After the case occurred, Chen instructed his friend Wu Qi and his clan brother Xinbo to meet with Yongyi in the Third District, induce him to enter the city, falsely claiming to be under the order of his uncle Gu Yongji, and trick him back to the Gu residence in Mao Xu Dun. He was imprisoned in a secret room by Wu and others. Wu then drafted a statement to withdraw the case and forged Yongyi's signature, submitting it to the county government to falsely withdraw the charges. However, after Yongyi escaped, he personally wrote a statement denying the forged withdrawal and requested that the case be handled strictly according to the law.

Robbery Occurs Outside Wangjiang Gate, Hangzhou 119

At Zhu Youfu's house, No. 8 Datong Bridge outside Wangjiang Gate in Hangzhou, four robbers suddenly came last night (30th) at midnight. They broke in with a wooden club and several bayonets, and robbed more than 240 yuan in cash and banknotes, a gold ring, and twelve dimes. The robbers fled towards Guantang.

Li Junpu Arrested for Extortion 120

Li Junpu, originally named Zou Fengchen, a native of Nanjing, residing at No. 77 Guan Lane, Hangzhou, is 25 years old. He graduated from university and has recently been unemployed. He conceived a bizarre idea and repeatedly wrote threatening letters to Wang Zhuzhai, chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Jin Runquan, president of the Bank of China, and Wang Xiangquan, president of the Pawn Industry Bank, demanding huge sums of money without success. The day before yesterday, he demanded 3,000 yuan from Zhang Xinpei, head of the Health Section of the Municipal Government, and was reported to the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau. Detective Wu Rongzhao and six others from the Detective Team went to wait and arrested the suspect Li Junpu. Team leader Zhu Xiaodong and squad leaders Tang Shihhu and Zhang Yongji jointly interrogated him. Li confessed to everything.

Three Deaths in a Family in Xiaoshan Due to Epidemic 121

Recently, the weather has been extremely hot and epidemics are rampant. On the 29th, in Sun Duanfu's family in Hui 　 Bridge outside the East Gate, a case of enteritis epidemic was discovered. That morning, his daughter died of the epidemic. In the afternoon, his wife also contracted the epidemic and died in the evening. On the 30th, his grandson also contracted the epidemic and his condition was serious. He was immediately treated by the Jimin Hospital, but died in less than four hours. There is still a seven-year-old child, and it is unknown how to avoid infection.

Bengbu Establishes an Epidemic Prevention Association 122

During this hot season, epidemics are most likely to spread. The Anhui Provincial Government previously issued a special order to all counties to establish epidemic prevention agencies to prevent the spread of epidemics. After receiving the order, the Public Security Bureau here immediately began preparations. On the afternoon of the 29th, Bureau Chief He Guoliang invited people from all walks of life to hold a meeting at the Sanmin Education Center at 3:00 PM to discuss organizational methods. It was decided to establish the Bengbu Summer Epidemic Prevention Committee, and 43 well-known local figures were appointed as epidemic prevention committee members. Currently, they are working hard to plan the internal organization and epidemic prevention measures. Once the funds are raised, they plan to establish an epidemic prevention isolation hospital and inspection station to prevent the spread of epidemics. Since the beginning of summer, no true epidemic has occurred in this city. In addition, with continuous cloudy and rainy weather, the temperature is cool. According to general speculation, there may not be a widespread epidemic this summer.

New Guidelines for Municipal Facilities in the Future 123

Mayor Wu Reported at the Municipal Government Memorial Week, Emphasizing Efforts to Cultivate People's Self-Governance Abilities to Gradually Transition from Official Governance to People's Governance - Central News Agency reports: This morning, the Municipal Government held a memorial week, attended by more than 100 officials from various bureaus and offices. Mayor Wu Tiecheng presided over the ceremony. Mayor Wu began by reporting on the new guidelines for future municipal facilities. The following is the speech delivered by Mayor Wu: Esteemed comrades, the most important legacy of the late Premier is construction. The purpose of our revolution is also construction.

Construction Work 124

In addition to people's livelihood construction and economic construction, political construction is especially important. During this period of political tutelage, all comrades in the Party, whether working in administrative agencies or Party headquarters, or serving in various professions locally, should lead the people of the whole country to jointly complete the political construction of the political tutelage period. The foundation of political construction lies in local self-government. Therefore, if local self-government work cannot be completed, the foundation of democracy cannot be consolidated. If the foundation of democracy cannot be consolidated, the purpose of political construction cannot be achieved. Therefore, since the "January 28th Incident" last year, after suffering severe damage, the Municipal Government, despite its extremely strained finances, has strived to prepare

Local Self-Government 125

work according to the original self-government procedures, and has also organized a Provisional Municipal Council. Although the councilors of the Provisional Municipal Council are nominated rather than elected, their powers are the same as those of a formally elected Municipal Council. Therefore, the entire Municipal Government should respect the Provisional Municipal Council as it would respect a democratically elected Municipal Council. This is a necessary stage in the process of preparing for self-government during the period of political tutelage. Our efforts to prepare for self-government work must aim at realizing democracy. We should not be like those who prepared for self-government in the past – district chiefs, local gentry, and headmen – who, after receiving orders from the central government, only put up a sign of preparing for self-government without any actual results. Our country has been in a state of instability for years. The work of preparing for self-government has been interrupted and resumed from time to time due to various changes. Therefore, although local self-government has been prepared for several times, it has not yet succeeded, and the foundation of local self-government has not been established. Therefore, my colleagues in the Municipal Government, based on past experiences, should not only enthusiastically prepare for local self-government, but also reflect on the shortcomings and mistakes of past preparations for local self-government, and use all our energy to

Strive Forward 126

The preparation procedures must be very strict and practical, so that our efforts to implement the preparation of local self-government can produce results. This is what we should pay attention to when implementing local self-government. Furthermore, the best place to implement local self-government is in cities, because cities are where talent is more concentrated, transportation facilities are more complete, and it is also an economic center. Therefore, implementing local self-government in cities is easier than in other inland areas, because cities are more equipped with the conditions for self-government. Therefore, comrades who serve in cities should work together to complete the work of local self-government, so that the political tutelage work of local self-government can succeed in cities, and at the same time, it can arouse interest in political construction throughout the country. Therefore, whenever the Municipal Government has the opportunity to allow local people to

Participate in Municipal Affairs 127

we try our best to give it to the local people. For example, the Municipal Bank is a bank run by the Municipal Government, but many directors and supervisors of the Municipal Bank are appointed from local leaders, so that they can participate in all the bank's operations. Also, like the Industrial and Trust Company that we are going to establish recently, we also want to invite local leaders and big businessmen to serve as directors and supervisors. There are also several other things, such as the Municipal Library, the Municipal Museum, and the Municipal Hospital, etc. We also want to invite local people to participate in the preparations. Not only to participate in the preparations, but after the establishment in the future, we will also invite local people to organize a board of directors to manage various undertakings. In short, our new guidelines for municipal facilities in the future are always to give local people more opportunities to participate in municipal affairs, so that municipal affairs can gradually progress from official governance to people's governance. Therefore, various public undertakings in the locality should not only invite local people to participate during the initial establishment or preparation period, but also

Proceed Together 128

but also hand them over to local people for management after they are established, so that these public welfare undertakings related to all citizens of the city will not be affected by political or personnel changes. Therefore, from now on, the Shanghai Municipal Government will follow this policy and direction and work hard to achieve the goal of transitioning from official governance to people's governance and realize the ideal of political construction.

Today's August 1st Anniversary 129

Chinese and Concession Police Agencies Declare Temporary Martial Law Today, August 1st, is the World Anti-Imperialist and Anti-War Movement Day. Every year on this day, workers' groups in countries around the world are expected to hold demonstrations and marches. In order to prevent reactionary elements from taking the opportunity to cause trouble, the Chinese and Concession police agencies in this city have declared a temporary state of martial law.

Temporary Martial Law 130

Wen Hong'en, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, ordered all district police stations, supervisory offices, and detective teams yesterday to implement temporary martial law today. All major roads will have double sentries, and supervisors and detectives will be fully deployed. The patrol teams of the Garrison Headquarters will continue to patrol as usual. The security teams under the Municipal Security Office will continue to be stationed in various places to guard the security of various districts. The police stations in the Public Concession and the French Concession have also been ordered to strengthen their defenses and deploy additional Chinese and Western armed detectives to guard the areas of worker schools in eastern and western Shanghai to prevent any incidents.

Gatherings and Meetings Prohibited 131

In addition to being ordered to declare temporary martial law, all Chinese and Concession police agencies have prohibited any gatherings, associations, marches, or demonstrations by workers and students. However, gatherings permitted by the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Committee, after prior notification to the district office in charge, will be provided with police protection; otherwise, they will also be prohibited. Yesterday, reactionary slogans written in chalk were found on the walls of Xujiahui Road, Pudong Yangshupu Road, and western Shanghai's Rue Robert streets in the French Concession. The authorities have paid special attention to strict investigation.

Ministry of Finance Streamlines Salt Tax 132

Construction of Salt Mounds in Northern Anhui Expected to Be Completed This Year - Stepped-up Training for Tax Police to Strictly Prevent Smuggling - Since the Seizure of Customs Revenue in Northeast China, the National Treasury's Revenue Has Been Greatly Reduced. In Order to Consolidate National Treasury Revenue, Minister of Finance Song Ziwen Has Begun to Streamline Salt Tax to Make Up for the Loss. He Visited Salt Areas in Northern Anhui by Plane This Spring with Zhu Tingqi, Director of the Salt Affairs Inspection Office, and Planned to Build More Salt Mounds, All of Which Have Been Set in Motion. A Central News Agency Reporter Recently Inquired with the Salt Industry in This City About the Latest Developments in the Ministry of Finance's Streamlining of Salt Affairs, As Follows:

Construction of Salt Mounds 133

The four salt fields of Banzhong and Linji in northern Anhui produce a large amount of salt. The scattered salt, which cannot be stored in mounds, amounts to tens of millions of dan each year. It is necessary to build a large number of salt mounds to concentrate the salt and prevent smuggling. Construction has already begun. The completed ones include Sanyanggang Official Mound, Renzhuang Mound, Huangsha Mound, and Xiakou Mound in Linxing Field, and Taiping Commercial Mound in Banpu Field, and Zhongzheng Commercial Mound in Zhongzheng Field. Those expected to be completed this year include Nanbei Mound, Zhizi Mound, Baisitou Mound, Lijiagang Mound, Kuangdongsha Mound, Liangdongsha Mound, Xingzhuang Mound, Wudonghe Mound, and Anjiazhuang Mound in Linxing Field, Houzui Mound and Dapu Commercial Mound in Banpu Field, Dongzoushan Official Mound and Zhang 　 Official Mound in Zhongzheng Field, and Chenjiagang Official Mound, Duigougang Official Mound, and Yanweigang Official Mound in Jinan Field. The cost of building the mounds and dredging the rivers is a total of 1,409,280 yuan.

Streamlining Tax Rates 134

Domestic salt sales areas have unequal tax rates in various regions. Although there were reasons for the regulations in the past, they were not originally intended to be high or low. However, the disparity is too great, and after a long time, smuggling is inevitable. Minister of Finance Song Ziwen, in view of this, ordered the General Inspectorate to streamline the tax rates in order to equalize the burden and increase tax revenue. After discussion, the General Inspectorate decided to raise the tax rates in all low-tax areas and not to increase the tax rates in high-tax areas for the time being. For adjacent areas, the tax rates will be increased or decreased to ensure balance. The various central and local surcharges, which are confusing and difficult to assess, have also been discussed and consolidated. The field tax and central surcharge paid in the producing area are collectively called the regular tax, and the shore tax and central surcharge paid at the sales area are called the sales tax. The local surcharges are called surcharges (except for the foreign debt surcharge, which is specifically set up to compensate for the pound sterling loss, which will remain the same). A temporary tax rate table for streamlining salt tax has been set up to streamline the process.

Tax Revenue Statistics 135

The total tax revenue statistics for the Republic of China in 1932 was 156,921,000 yuan, including 22,126,000 yuan from Changlu, 2,632,000 yuan from Hedong, 469,000 yuan from Koubei, 977,000 yuan from Jinbei, 7,942,000 yuan from Shandong, 12,447,000 yuan from Huaibei, 13,763,000 yuan from Yangzhou, 9,250,000 yuan from Songjiang, 9,862,000 yuan from Liangzhe, 12,777,000 yuan from E'an, 13,549,000 yuan from Xiang'an, 5,203,000 yuan from Wan'an, 7,970,000 yuan from Xi'an, 5,371,000 yuan from Henan, 3,847,000 yuan from Fujian, 10,483,000 yuan from Guangdong, 1,622,000 yuan from Guangxi, 2,043,000 yuan from Yunnan, 2,581,000 yuan from South Sichuan, 1,905,000 yuan from North Sichuan, 337,000 yuan from Gansu, 83,000 yuan from Qinghai, 295,000 yuan from Xinjiang, 387,000 yuan from Ningxia, and 291,000 yuan from Lianyun sales abroad, totaling 157,212,000 yuan.

Training of Tax Police 136

The training of tax police is extremely important. In the past, smuggling squads were often understaffed and had bad habits, extorting money and releasing smugglers. Therefore, strict screening was carried out during the reorganization, vacancies were filled, and training was stepped up to create an elite force. Since the establishment of the Tax Police Section and the Water Patrol Unit, the affiliated patrol ships have been reorganized. The original eight patrol ships and two steamers have also been repaired separately, so that land and water joint defense can easily prevent smuggling. The tax police achieved significant results in suppressing smuggling, seizing a total of 64,148 dan and 87 jin of smuggled goods last year.

Aviation Highway Construction Lottery Drawn Yesterday 150

Representatives from All Sectors Inspect Aircraft Soaring in Celebration - First Prize Not Sold - Redrawn as Special Prize - Special Prize Number 299287 - Winning Tickets Can Be Redeemed at Three Banks in Seven Days

丨Winner of the First Prize Still Unidentified丨 151

The first aviation highway construction lottery issued by the National Government, totaling 500,000 numbers, has been enthusiastically purchased by all sectors since its launch, which is unprecedented. This is because the profits from this lottery are used for national construction, and the chances of winning a prize are higher than other lotteries. Yesterday was the date of the first lottery draw, which was held at the Yiyuan in the French Concession on Albert Road at 1:00 PM. About 10,000 representatives from all parties and Chinese and foreign citizens went to visit. At the same time, there were three airplanes flying in the sky above the 　 . At 1:15 PM, the lottery draw began in public and continued until 8:20 PM. The winning lottery numbers and the various circumstances of the lottery draw are summarized below:

The Scene When the First Prize Was Drawn (Photo by Wang Kai　　)

Layout of the Venue 152

The lottery venue was set up in front of the grandstand on the front side of the dog racing track in the garden. The layout of the venue was very simple. A bamboo shed was set up under the grandstand, with three copper balls, A, B, and C, inside. Ball B was the largest and set in the center. A and B were smaller and set on the left and right sides as recording tables 　 . The middle was the prize draw and announcement area, with two phonographs. The grandstand opposite was for the seats of the supervisory committee members and representatives from all sectors, Chinese and foreign reporters, etc. The rest were for the audience seats for Chinese and foreign citizens. Inside and outside the venue, the French police sent detectives to maintain order and posted signs such as "Welcome to Visit."

Supervision from All Sectors 153

In addition to the presence of Chinese and foreign supervisors, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Banking Association and other organizations also sent representatives to supervise the venue. The committee members included Qian Xinzhi, Dong XianGuang, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai (represented by Sun Luping), Yu Qiaqing, 　 Yanfang, Ye Zhuo　, Hu Yunqiu, and Hu Bijian. Chairman's Speech 154

Before the drawing, Chairman Song Ziwen first delivered a speech on behalf of Zhang Yong, roughly stating: "Today is the day for the first issuance of aviation and highway construction lottery tickets by the National Government, and we are very pleased to see such good results. If the people are all enthusiastic about the government's aviation and highway construction, then the hope of success is promising. At the same time, we can also see the greatness of the spirit of cooperation between the people and the government. Therefore, we firmly believe that the issuance of the second and third lottery tickets in the future will surely achieve even better results. Today, I represent the government to thank you all and also thank the enthusiasm of the people involved in this event. There is still one point that must be clarified to you. It must be drawn from the sold lottery ticket numbers. Now that the time has arrived, the drawing will begin on time." (Translated into English by Dong Guoen)

Details of the Drawing 155

The chairman personally attended the scene to supervise. First, the small balls and ball plate of Machine B were opened for inspection one by one. Then, they were poured into Machine B in three separate batches. Subsequently, Machines C and A were also poured in successively. Then, the three machines were shaken simultaneously, shaken a total of three times. Then, the spring doors were opened, and the numbers jumped out. The announcer called out the numbers and grades, and then the recorder registered them. At the same time, the numbers were posted and announced. This was done in rotation until 8:30 PM. The announcers and number runners all wore white spun silk long gowns, and both hands were covered with white hard half-sleeve gloves. When picking up the numbers, they raised their hands high to show that there was no selfishness or fraud.

Shanghai Machinery Manufacturers Joint Association Sends Another Letter to the Ratepayers Association Regarding the Municipal Council's Warning to Factories 161

The Municipal Council should be fully responsible for the damage to the factories caused by the erroneous investigation. Xin Sheng News Agency reports that regarding the Municipal Council's warning to various factories, the Shanghai Machinery Manufacturers Joint Association (機聯會) yesterday sent another letter to the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Shanghai International Settlement, requesting assistance. Details are as follows:

Letter to the Ratepayers Association 162

The Shanghai Machinery Manufacturers Joint Association wrote to the Ratepayers Association yesterday, stating: "Regarding the fact that the concession authorities unilaterally amended Article 34 of the Yangjingbang Regulations, authorizing the Municipal Council to do so, and the Municipal Council used Article 30, which has been in place for a long time, as an excuse to inspect factories, regardless of the background or whether it is a seizure of power, we will put it aside for now. The Association believes that Chinese factories are simple and crude, and their safety equipment must be immature. However, within its sphere of influence, the Municipal Council uses the guise of preventing public danger. The conclusion of our Association's July 15th declaration even indicated that we would assist the Municipal Council in avoiding criticism and instruct factories. The so-called gentleman can be deceived by his way. Moreover, the Municipal Council sends Westerners to investigate factories. If our factory's contents are complete, there should be a Western-speaking staff member to deal with them. Otherwise, if the Municipal Council relies solely on the Western investigator's own ideals for speculation and then warns the factory to stop, is it inappropriate? This is very questionable. Judging from the warning received by the Yisheng Rubber Factory this time, two errors were found, which made us even more suspicious. The errors are briefly described below: (1) The rubber factory's refining and grinding are essentially one type of work, but after the investigator's investigation, the Municipal Council's warning letter actually divided them into two. (2) The rubber factory's shoe-hanging cart and freight cart are completely different. According to the shoe-hanging cart, the pushing cannot be forceful, because if you use force, the luster of the overshoes will be lost. However, after the investigator's investigation, the Municipal Council's warning letter stated that methods should be found to avoid the use of hard tools on iron products. The iron freight cars traveling on iron rails should not have wheels with iron or hard edges. Therefore, we issued Notice No. 504 to our members yesterday. If you receive an English letter from the Municipal Council, you should return it immediately and ask them to translate it into Chinese, and send it together with the original English letter, so as to avoid one mistake leading to another. However, the Municipal Council does not hire specialized personnel to conduct investigations, and the matter is not taken seriously. If the factory suffers significant losses due to an erroneous investigation, the Municipal Council should be fully responsible for compensating the losses. We are concerned that your Association, as the highest body representing more than 55% of the tax revenue and more than 95% of the population in the International Settlement, hereby inform you specially, respectfully requesting you to investigate and make a strong statement to avoid errors and disputes."

Hoping to Avoid Errors 163

Yesterday, Cheng Shouzhong, Secretary-General of the Machinery Manufacturers Joint Association, told the Xin Sheng News Agency reporter: "Our Association is assisting the Municipal Council to guide factories and improve their contents to avoid public danger, so that the lives and property of citizens can be guaranteed safety. We are willing to run between the Municipal Council and the factories under the scorching sun to seek simple and direct improvement methods and avoid major setbacks and losses due to shutdowns and factory relocations. The Municipal Council's meticulousness in handling affairs has long been recognized by the citizens, not just by our Association. However, due to assisting Yisheng Factory to improve its interior, after many days of research with its manager and factory director, it was found that there were two errors in the Municipal Council's warning to Yisheng Rubber Factory. Therefore, I, together with the manager and factory director of Yisheng Factory, went to the Municipal Council on the 29th of the month. In addition to bringing two official letters replying to the Municipal Council's warning from Yisheng First Factory and Yisheng Second Factory, and stating the points of improvement, we also told Mr. He Dejun, the joint officer, that in addition to the two errors, we have sent a letter to the Chinese Ratepayers Association to file a protest, and asked him to convey these errors to the person in charge of the Municipal Council. He accepted our request. Our Association has now sent a letter to the Ratepayers Association, requesting them to make a strong statement to avoid errors."

The 12th Group of Displaced Refugees from Mexico Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning 164

Zhu Zigao and six others will arrive soon. The refugees who have been obstructed are in urgent need of relief to return to their country. Xin Xin News Agency reports that the 12th group of displaced refugees who were expelled from Mexico arrived in Shanghai at 8:30 AM yesterday, aboard the President Monroe of the Da Lai Company. The Global Overseas Chinese General Association and the Mexican Refugee Relief Association sent representatives Fang Difei, Huang Zhulin, Chen Hanbin, Lin Wenqi, and more than ten others to the Da Lai Wharf in Baizijing, Pudong, to greet them. They rested at the meeting hall on Guizhou Road. This time, only six people, including Zhu Zigao, Liu Guang, Zhu Yiji, Xie Lian (from Taishan), Situ Shu, and Hu Huang (from Kaiping), arrived in Shanghai due to insufficient berths on the President Monroe. According to Zhu Zigao's statement to the Xin Xin News Agency reporter, Mexico refused to subsidize the refugees' travel expenses to return to China, and the U.S. government stopped providing supplies to avoid huge losses and ordered to prohibit refugees from smuggling into the U.S. After that, more than 10,000 refugees remaining in Mexico are unable to return to their country due to lack of travel expenses and are subject to humiliation by the anti-Chinese party. Their inner pain can be imagined. They urgently hope that the government will take measures to provide relief as soon as possible to avoid being stranded in foreign countries. As for the rest who were able to return to China this time, it was because they were detained in the U.S. before the ban. There are still ten people in the U.S. waiting for the ship, and they will be able to return to China one after another soon. It is also heard that Zhu Zigao and the other six are scheduled to take the original ship to Hong Kong this morning to return to their ancestral home in Guangdong. The Overseas Chinese General Association will provide temporary relief funds of ten yuan per person as usual.

Shanghai Telephone Bureau Revises Public Telephone Prices 166

The Shanghai Telephone Bureau sent a letter to the Municipal Public Works Bureau, stating: "In order to facilitate public calls, our bureau has approved various businesses inside and outside the city to install public telephones at appropriate locations. The applicants are responsible for their own management, and all installation fees, deposits, and long-distance Chinese and foreign registration fees are waived. It has been found that there are more than 50 public telephones that have been installed. According to the cost calculation of common telephone equipment and line materials, each call requires 3.5 cents. Currently, the fee for each local call is 3 cents, which seems to be a loss based on the cost calculation. Since the use of automatic machines, the capital investment has increased significantly, and the cost of each call should be slightly increased to compensate. All public telephone prices should be revised accordingly. The Ministry of Communications' Directive No. 9152 has been approved and will be implemented from August 1st. All local calls between Nanshi, Zhabei, Jiangwan, Longhua, Pudong, the concession, and Zhenru and Wusong, as well as local calls between public telephones in the Nanshi, Zhabei, Jiangwan, Longhua, and other districts, and calls between public telephones in this district and other districts, will be changed to 5 cents per call."

Employees and Workers of the Shanghai Power Company Jointly Petition the Municipal Council 167

Demanding the protection of the work of former Electrical Department employees and the improvement of treatment. Seven requests were made to negotiate with the company. The workers of the Shanghai Power Company demanded the reinstatement of the work of union director Ni Wenfu and others, as well as four treatment conditions, but the results were not obtained. A few days ago, the entire group petitioned the Municipal Party Department. At the same time, the employees of the company also made the same request. Yesterday, they jointly petitioned the Municipal Council with worker representatives, requesting assistance, and submitted a proposal to protect the employees of the former Electrical Department and a proposal to improve treatment, requesting that they be forwarded to the company for negotiation. The details are recorded separately as follows:

Joint Petition 168

The Shanghai Power Company Employees' Mutual Benefit Association (i.e., the one organized by employees) sent representatives Wu Zupei and Cao Xingbei, together with worker representatives Ni Wenfu, Pan Genlin, Chen Baogen, and Zhang Caisheng, to the Municipal Council General Office on Jiangxi Road at 10:30 AM yesterday, carrying letters of petition. They were met by Joint Officer He Dejun, who first listened to the representatives state their intention to request assistance. He responded that their letter had been fully explained to General Officer Zhong Si, but the Municipal Council needed to consider the case in detail, so he could not reply today, but he hoped to have another opportunity to talk in a short period of time to achieve a satisfactory solution. The representatives were satisfied and left.

Letter to the Municipal Council 169

The original letter from the Shanghai Power Company Employees' Appeal Association to the Municipal Council stated: "We, the undersigned, have served in your Electrical Department for many years. After being taken over by the Shanghai Power Company in 1929, our positions were guaranteed by Mr. O'Shea, the manager of your Electrical Department, and we continued to serve in the Power Company. He also guaranteed that our positions would be as secure as if they were under the name of the Municipal Council. However, recently, the Power Company has continued to lay off employees of the former Electrical Department, causing us great panic. On June 21st, we sent a letter to Mr. Sheard, the general manager of the Power Company, asking him to pay attention, but we have not received a reply so far. We have repeatedly requested the company to improve our treatment due to the needs of the current environment, but we have been repeatedly rejected, and even four of the directors of our legally organized trade union have been suspended. Therefore, the masses are indignant and resentful. Therefore, after the decision of the general meeting of all employee representatives, we respectfully request that your bureau, based on the friendship between the former host and guests, forward the attached proposals for protecting the employees of the former Electrical Department and improving treatment to the Power Company as soon as possible, and earnestly guarantee our status and future as if they were under the name of the Municipal Council. We believe that your bureau will have sympathy and assistance for the personnel of the former Electrical Department who have contributed to it. We have sent representatives to visit and hope to be granted an audience and to be instructed in everything. We salute you, Zhong, the General Officer of the Municipal Council of the International Settlement."

Letter to the Company 170

"We respectfully inform you that we sent you a letter on June 22nd regarding the company's unreasonable layoffs, but we have not received a reply. As for the workers' request to improve treatment, we have repeatedly requested it, but the company has turned a deaf ear to it. Therefore, the masses are indignant. Therefore, after the decision of the general meeting of employee representatives, we respectfully request that you accept and implement the proposals for protecting the employees transferred from the former Electrical Department and improving treatment. We will be very fortunate. We salute you, Mr. Huo, President of the Power Company, and Mr. Sheard, General Manager of the Power Company. Attached are proposals for protecting employees and improving treatment. The Shanghai Power Company Employees' Appeal Association."

Seven Conditions 171

The employees and workers of the company jointly proposed a total of seven items for improving treatment. The original text is as follows: (1) All employees who have served in the company for more than one year shall be given a year-end bonus of one month's salary at the end of each year. (Note) The China Merchants Electrical Company's year-end bonus is two months, and 50% of the surplus is used as a bonus. (2) All employees who have served in the company for more than one year shall receive three months' severance pay and 5% of the accumulated labor fund when they are laid off by the company, regardless of whether they are dismissed for cause or without cause. (Except for those who have been convicted of criminal acts related to the company by a court) They should also receive 5% of the accumulated labor fund. (Note) The British American Tobacco Company gives 5% to those who resign voluntarily and 10% to those who are laid off by the company. If there is a criminal act, the money is still paid even if they have been prosecuted. (3) All employees who have served in the company for more than one year shall be entitled to two weeks of annual leave (limited to employees). (Note) The current Chinese staff of the Municipal Council has three weeks of annual leave each year, and the senior Chinese staff of the Power Company also have two weeks of annual leave each year. (4) All employees who have served in the company for more than one year and are ordered to retire due to illness by a doctor shall be given 5% of the accumulated labor fund and an additional 5% of the sick retirement fund. (5) When an employee who has served in the company for more than one year dies, he/she shall receive 5% of the accumulated labor fund, 5% of the pension, and 60 yuan for funeral expenses. Those who die on duty shall be given a special pension of 2,000 yuan. Those who are disabled on duty shall be paid their original salary until the date of their death. (Note) The British American Tobacco Company gives a special pension of 1,500 yuan to those who die on duty. (6) If a worker is sick, his/her medical expenses shall be borne by the company in addition to the salary being paid as usual. (Note) The British American Tobacco Company pays the salary as usual when a worker is sick, and the medical expenses are borne by the company. Currently, the salary of a worker who is sick at the Power Company is reduced by half. If they are hospitalized, the medical expenses are borne by the worker himself. For example, if the worker's salary is 60 cents a day, the company only pays half, 30 cents. How will the worker pay for medical expenses? If the doctor tells the worker to be hospitalized and he/she does not comply, the salary will not be paid at all. (7) Increase the salary increase rate set in 1930. (Note) In 1930, the company had been in operation for less than a year, and the original salary increase rate of the Municipal Council was reduced, and there were grades and other restrictions. For example, the monthly salary of a newly hired employee is 27.5 yuan. After one year of service, one yuan is added, up to 37.5 yuan as one level. If he/she does not receive special praise up to 37.5 yuan, the salary increase will stop. New workers receive 68 cents per day, with an annual increase of one cent, up to 80 cents. If they do not get promoted, it will stop forever. This salary increase method is not in line with the evolution of modern life. (Additional rules) 1. Subsidize the monthly fee for the employees' club. 2. Reinstate the four union directors who were dismissed. 3. Establish a school for employees' children. 4. Reorganize the medical office. There must be resident doctors on Fielun Road and Yangshupu Road. It is forbidden to use waste paper and newspaper to wrap medicines to value human life.

How Can the Shanghai Municipal Council's Tax Collectors Abuse and Insult Taxpayers? 176

丨The Chinese Taxpayers' Association Sends a Letter Requesting the Shanghai Municipal Council to Rectify the Situation.丨 Yesterday, regarding the abuse and insults of taxpayers by the Shanghai Municipal Council's tax collectors, the Chinese Taxpayers' Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council, stating: Respectfully, according to a letter from taxpayer Xu Jizhuang, a Western tax collector and a Chinese tax collector were dispatched by the Shanghai Municipal Council at 11:00 AM today (the 28th) to collect taxes at Jiaheli, Hart Road. However, the taxpayer had not received prior notification from the Shanghai Municipal Council. Furthermore, as the taxpayer is a member of the military, his salary is paid out at the beginning of each month. However, the Western tax collector pressed him urgently, added insults, and said he would come to collect the tax the next morning. The taxpayer stated that tomorrow would be the same as today, and requested to pay the tax on August 10th. However, in addition to the insults, the Western tax collector also struck the taxpayer's face with his fists, and stated that he would come to collect the tax the next morning. The taxpayer stated that the matter concerns being insulted and disturbed, and if this continues, the residents will be humiliated beyond what is bearable. The taxpayer truthfully reported this and requested your council to handle it impartially, and to inform the Shanghai Municipal Council to avoid the above situation from happening again in the future, and to provide formal prior notice when collecting taxes. Based on this, the collection of municipal general taxes is divided into four seasons each year, with each season lasting three months. At the beginning of each season, the collection should be handled in the same way as Western-style residences to avoid disputes arising from discriminatory treatment. Later, in order to save money, your council pre-published tax payment notices in various newspapers. Although tax payment notices were not issued in advance, it was indeed equally effective. However, this has not been followed for long, and is no longer being done. Since the municipal general tax is collected every three months, the period from the first day of the first month to the end of the third month is the time for paying taxes. Now, if what taxpayer Xu Jizhuang said is true, he did not refuse to pay the tax, nor did he fail to pay it on time, and only requested to pay it on August 10th, which is a normal request. However, the tax collector abused his position and acted recklessly and insultingly, which is extremely inappropriate. Based on the above, we are writing to request that you investigate and instruct the tax collection office to rectify the situation. This is addressed to the General Manager of the Shanghai Municipal Council for the Shanghai International Settlement.

Customs to Formulate Measures for Inspecting Foreigners' Entry Passports 177

Regarding the punishment of foreign ships, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs should first conduct thorough consultations with relevant countries before it can be implemented without obstruction. Regarding the issue of amending the inspection of foreigners' entry passports, the Inspector General of Customs, after receiving the order from the Customs Administration, immediately drafted measures to assist in the implementation and submitted them to the authorities for approval. The original report is recorded below: The Customs should do its best to inspect foreigners' entry passports to ensure that the measures are effectively implemented. However, after carefully examining the points of amendment discussed by the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, there seem to be difficulties in implementation because

Extraterritoriality 178

has not yet been abolished. For cases of violations by foreigners enjoying extraterritoriality and foreign shipping companies, the Customs, based on treaty provisions and the severity of the circumstances, handles them separately on the grounds of protecting tax revenue. Foreign merchants also pay the fines in full without any objection because the treaty stipulates different penalties for smuggling, including confiscation of cargo ships. However, if the punishment is not related to tax revenue, it will

Invoke the Treaty 179

as there are no relevant provisions. The consul of that country will file a protest, leading to negotiations. Therefore, regarding the punishment of foreign ships, I believe that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs must first conduct thorough consultations with relevant countries, and only after obtaining their consent can it be implemented without obstruction. As for the provision that foreigners coming to China without a passport should be ordered to be carried back by the shipping company, it is also quite difficult to implement before the countries concerned have agreed. However, in practice, there seems to be no need for such a provision because

Foreigners Entering 180

without a passport, or with a passport that has not been certified by our embassy, and without a legitimate reason, our country cannot allow them to disembark. Since they are not allowed to disembark, the shipping company will have to carry them elsewhere. There is no need to specify that the shipping company should be responsible for carrying them back. According to international practice, when shipping companies sell tickets, they first require passengers to sign a statement certifying that their passports and other documents are complete before they can sell them, so as to avoid losses for the company. Therefore,

Our Authorities 181

only need to notify the foreign shipping companies to submit passenger lists to the Customs when the ships arrive at the port, according to the procedure for submitting passenger lists to the Customs, and stipulate that passengers are not allowed to embark or disembark without special permission from our country before their passports have been verified. Then, passengers can wait for verification in order and will not try to avoid it and disembark privately. If the company approves and passengers disembark privately, it can be discussed with the countries concerned to impose

Appropriate Punishment. 182

As for the method of ordering shipping companies to submit passenger lists, it has already been implemented in Shanghai. It is expected that there will be no difficulty in promoting it to other ports. If there are those who refuse to submit them, the Customs can order them to submit an extra copy in addition to the one submitted to the Customs, which will be forwarded by the Customs for record. All the difficulties in implementing the methods discussed by the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to assist in punishing foreign merchant shipping companies for violations have been clarified.

Social Bureau and French Concession Police to Conduct Second Inspection of Weights and Measures Starting Today 183

The promotion of the new system of weights and measures in this city has long been declared unified, with a set schedule for inspections to be conducted in stages and on a daily basis. However, due to special circumstances in the concession areas, the Municipal Social Bureau and the French Concession Police have mutually agreed to implement the first inspection two years ago, which only covered a portion of the area. The inspection was interrupted due to the Shanghai War. It is now reported that the bureau and others, in accordance with the agreement, have sent a letter to the French Concession Police to conduct a second inspection of factories, shops, and vegetable markets, starting on August 1st. The French Concession Police's reply and the inspection schedule are recorded below.

Police Reply 184

Respectfully, regarding the letter from your director to the French Municipal Council on July 5th, the inspection of weights and measures has already been ordered to the police stations under this office to carry out this matter to the best of their ability. In accordance with the agreement between the Chinese and French authorities on November 27, 1931, your bureau's inspectors should first contact the police station before starting their inspection. The police officers of this office are responsible for accompanying the inspectors and assisting them during the inspection, and for confiscating any non-compliant weights and measures. If there are any cases that should be prosecuted, this office will formally file a complaint based on the responsible authorities of your country. To facilitate the proposed inspection, please notify your director of the routes and times a few days in advance. This is addressed to Wu, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau, Faber.
