The New Building of the Kuo Hua Commercial Bank is Completed 186

The 11-story building built by the bank will be moved into today for business. The existing location of the Kuo Hua Commercial Bank on Ningbo Road is no longer sufficient for business development. Therefore, the bank purchased a site at the corner of Beijing Road and Henan Road and built an 11-story building. After more than a year of construction, it was completed a few days ago. The bank will officially move into the new building for business today, which has attracted the attention of people in society. The bank authorities specially led guests to visit the new building yesterday. The results of the investigation are described as follows:

Brief History 187

The bank was founded by Zou Minchu, Tang Shoumin, and others. The head office is located in Shanghai and officially opened in July of the 17th year of the Republic of China, less than six years ago. The initial authorized capital was 2 million yuan, with half of it actually paid up. Later, as the business developed, the authorized capital increased to 4 million yuan, and the amount actually received has recently approached 3 million yuan, and is still being raised. In the past five years, branches have been established in Suzhou, Nanjing, Guangzhou, and Hongkou, Nanshi, and Xinzha in Shanghai. Offices have also been established in Xumen, Suzhou, Chengbei, Nanjing, and Hong Kong and Xiamen. Recently, a branch will be added in Baxianqiao in Shanghai, which will be opened within one or two months. It is heard that the bank has many contacts in Southeast Asia, and in the near future, it plans to gradually set up branches in important ports there.

Business Overview 188

The bank's current business is broadly divided into deposits, loans, remittances, savings, and trusts. Among them, savings and trusts are allocated separate funds and special departments are set up to handle them. Accounting and business are first divided independently, and the savings accounts are reported and published. The trust business includes the safekeeping of warehouses, real estate, and securities, which is quite developed. The amount of remittances made by the bank over the years is quite large, with a total of about 90 million yuan last year, with remittances to South China being the largest. The deposit business has also made progress. According to its first-quarter financial report this year, the total amount is close to 20 million yuan, an increase of almost five times compared with the bank's financial report in the 17th year of the Republic of China. It is not easy to achieve this in less than six years.

New Building Facilities 189

The bank's new building is located at the corner of Beijing Road and Henan Road, covering an area of nearly two acres and 11 stories high. The facade adopts the latest vertical line style, and the high tower on the front face pierces into the clouds, which is especially magnificent. The third floor and above are rented out as office space. The bank's own part, in addition to the land trial, occupies the ground floor, the mezzanine, and the second floor, a total of three floors. The ground floor is the business room, with counters on both sides and a passage in the middle. The communication office, deposit, remittance, branch receipt, and exchange of payments are located on the right, and the foreign exchange and savings departments are located on the left. At the end of the passage is a large escalator leading to the mezzanine, where the trust department and the vault are located. The vault and the book and evidence vault are located in the basement under the ground floor, and the layout is extremely well connected. The ground floor and the mezzanine are the location of the business department, so the decoration is as gorgeous as possible. The ground floor, walls, pillars, escalators, and counters are all paved with the finest Italian marble, which is dazzling. The flower glass ceiling on the roof is also very beautiful. The vault equipment on the mezzanine is sturdy, and the vault walls are all made of 18-inch thick steel and concrete, and the inner walls are all covered with steel plates. The vault door is made of 16-inch thick steel and is equipped with clock locks, secret switches, etc., which cannot be opened unless at a certain time. Thousands of safe deposit boxes are installed in the vault, all sizes are available, and the keys on the boxes are said to be the latest style, which is rare in Shanghai. All other facilities are very well-equipped to ensure the convenience and comfort of customers. The bank authorities have carefully planned, which is worthy of praise.

Complimentary Commemorative Album 190

The bank is moving into a new building for business and does not want to follow the trend of using gifts to attract customers. However, to commemorate the new building, it has specially collected information on commerce, economics, and daily social affairs, and compiled a book called "Daily Essentials," which is very exquisite in content and decoration. It will be given to customers for browsing and as a souvenir.

Bank of Communications Moves to New Location Today 191

The new location of the Bank of Communications at No. 16 North Henan Road has been decorated and will be moved into for business today. It is heard that in order to commemorate the relocation and give preferential treatment to depositors, all those who open a savings account with the bank today will receive an extra 1% interest and a beautiful gift.

Fire in Lloyd Road, Five People Escape by Jumping Out of Windows and are Injured 195

Yesterday afternoon at around 5:30 PM, a fire broke out accidentally in the upstairs of the Zhenxin Cigarette Paper Shop at No. 50, Deyu Lane, Lloyd Road, Tianjin Road. Suddenly, the flames soared and the fire was raging. It spread to the upper floors of No. 48, Yusenxiang Clothing Shop, No. 46, Qingmige Mounting Bookstore, No. 44, Large Pancake Shop, and Nos. 42 and 40, Xinchang Leather Shop. When the fire was raging, the residents upstairs of the Xinchang Leather Shop could not escape because the ladder was burned down. Five men and women jumped out of the windows one after another, and all were seriously injured as a result. They were Jin Li, an old woman from Haimen, 40 years old, with a broken left leg; Wang Yatang from Zhenjiang, 60 years old, with a broken right leg; Wang Bingsheng, 44 years old, from Zhejiang, with a broken right foot; Jin Alian from Haimen, 42 years old, with an injured left foot; and Chang Qinsheng, 33 years old, with burns on his face. They were sent to Renji Hospital for treatment by the Old Gate Police Station No. 116. At the fire scene, the fire brigade drove fire engines to put out the fire, which was extinguished until after 7:00 PM. A total of four houses were burned down. It is heard that Xinchang Leather Shop has fire insurance.

The Municipal Health Bureau Announces Reports on Infectious Diseases and Water Testing 197

丨Starting this month, reports will be issued weekly丨

The Municipal Health Bureau, considering that epidemics are likely to spread since the start of summer, has been actively carrying out various epidemic prevention measures. Starting this month (August), it will resume testing tap water in the city, starting with the two water districts of the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company and the Nanshi Chinese Business Water and Electricity Company. Each company has been asked to submit a detailed report on the composition and quality of the water produced daily. The Municipal Health Bureau will then randomly test the water. If there are any unclean or harmful ingredients, measures will be taken to ban and improve them. The test results will be reported to the public every week to ensure that the public is aware of and pays attention to prevention. At the same time, infectious disease testing and mortality reports will be carried out, and the state of epidemic diseases in the city will be announced to the public to raise awareness. The above two items have been published by the Health Bureau in the Shen, Xin, Shishi, Min, Chen, Shishi newspapers, and the English Continental Daily on a regular basis. The first issue has been decided to be published in the above newspapers tomorrow. All citizens are asked to pay attention. The water composition test and the names of infectious diseases tested are listed below: (A) (Infectious Diseases) Disease Names (1) Typhoid fever, (2) Paratyphoid fever, (3) Epidemic Typhus, (4) Diphtheria, (5) Smallpox, (6) Plague, (7) Cholera, (8) Bacillary and Amoebic Dysentery, (9) Epidemic Cerebrospinal Meningitis, (10) Scarlet Fever, (B) (Tap Water Testing) (1) Date of Collection, (2) Location of Water Sample, (3) Turbidity, (4) Total Mass, (5) Chloride Content, (6) Alkalinity, (7) Total Hardness, (8) Number of Bacteria per Cubic Centimeter Cultured at 37 Degrees Celsius for 24 Hours, (9) Coliform Bacteria, (10) Pathogens.

There is No Genuine Cholera in This City 202

The results of the examination showed no cholera germs. Citizens are encouraged to receive injections for prevention. Recently, reports stated that cholera had occurred in Caojiadu, Huxi, in this city. The Health Bureau sent personnel to conduct a thorough investigation and sent the feces of suspected cholera patients to the Health Laboratory for examination to clarify the situation. The examination results showed no cholera germs. The reports were false. Generally, citizens who have not studied medicine do not understand the scientific differentiation of symptoms. They often mistakenly attribute heatstroke or other causes of vomiting and diarrhea to cholera, leading to the spread of misinformation and sensational reports in newspapers. However, the Health Bureau is actively carrying out epidemic prevention during the summer and autumn seasons. Citizens are strongly encouraged to receive cholera vaccinations to increase their immunity to epidemics and to avoid drinking raw water or its mixtures. Fly eradication should be strictly implemented to prevent transmission.

New Plans for Japanese Shipping to China 203

Flourishing passenger transport between Shanghai and Japan leads to the addition of the "Omi Maru" to the route.

NYK Increases Ships 204

Recently, the passenger ships of the Nippon Yusen Kaisha (NYK) between Shanghai and Japan, namely the "Shanghai Maru" and "Nagasaki Maru," have been insufficient to meet the demand of passengers in Shanghai. The other six ships, including the "Rokko Maru," "Maya Maru," and "Aso Maru," only have third-class cabins and no first-class cabins. This has led to repeated instances of the "Shanghai Maru" and other ships being fully booked and tickets being returned. The Shanghai branch of the company has telegraphed the Tokyo head office requesting additional passenger ships on the Shanghai-Kobe-Osaka route to meet the demand. The head office has replied to Shanghai that the 4,200-ton passenger ship "Omi Maru," which sails to the South Sea Islands, will be added to the China-Japan route. The ship has first, second, and third-class cabins. The first sailing should arrive today, and it will then be dedicated to the Shanghai-Japan route. In the current sluggishness of shipping in various routes, the flourishing of the China-Japan route is truly a special situation.

Promoting Japanese Goods 205

Japanese people's efforts in promoting foreign trade are unmatched by those of other countries. In recent years, after the September 18th Incident, they have been affected by the boycott of Japanese goods in various parts of our country, leading to overproduction and stockpiles of goods. Although they can now be successively transported to various ports along our Yangtze River, purchasing power is minimal. The boycott of Japanese goods in various ports in Southeast Asia continues unabated. The Japanese have changed their strategy, transferring large quantities of Japanese goods to the South Seas Islands and West Africa for dumping at reduced prices. The Osaka Company and Mitsui & Co. have, at the request of various Japanese merchants, opened a new shipping route from Japan and Shanghai to Siam, specifically to transport Japanese goods to Siam. Currently, Osaka and Mitsui have each dispatched two ships to Siam.

Accepting Subsidies 206

The Nisshin Kisen Kaisha (Japanese Mail Steamship Company) in this port has suspended operations for a year and a half. Four ships operate on the Yangtze River, averaging less than one or two hundred tons of cargo per trip. Now that the Sino-Japanese war is over, Japanese businesses in China are seeking to recover. Nisshin is also requesting a subsidy of two million yuan from the government to revive the Yangtze River and North-South shipping routes. At the same time, President Baron Takashi Fukao has personally come to Shanghai to negotiate the resumption of services. Now that Fukao has returned to Tokyo, the Japanese government's subsidy to Nisshin has been approved by the Ministry of Communications for 970,000 Japanese yen. Now that the funds are available for collection, Nisshin's resumption plan will add more departures on the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River once the funds arrive.

Autumn House Tax in This City 207

The Finance Bureau Announces the Collection Starting Today. The City Finance Bureau issued Announcement No. 219 yesterday regarding the collection of the autumn house tax in this city: In order to collect the house tax, the city is divided into four seasons. The four collection offices in the east, south, west, and north of this bureau each assign collectors within their jurisdiction to collect the tax based on the house tax receipts. The paper color of these house tax receipts changes every quarter. The back of the receipt contains important information, and the front specifies the taxpayer's address, house number, and amount of tax paid. The receipt is stamped with the seal of this bureau to ensure its authenticity. This procedure has been in place for some time. Now, to strictly prevent the forgery of house tax receipts and eliminate malfeasance, starting from the collection of this year's autumn house tax, each page of the receipt will be perforated and stamped with the round seal of the respective collection office. Starting from August 1st, all collectors will wear uniforms when collecting taxes. Taxpayers may request to see the collector's identification card with their photograph affixed to it. If anyone is found carrying forged receipts and collecting tax fraudulently, they should be immediately handed over to the police. After this announcement, if taxpayers fail to verify the collector's identity and are deceived, the taxpayer will still be required to pay the house tax to maintain city tax revenue. This announcement is made to notify all relevant parties, including the municipal government and all collection offices of this bureau, for compliance.

Detective is Too Ignorant 208

Mistakenly Identifying a Respectable Woman as a Prostitute. Section Chief Yi from the First Branch of the First District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau Requests a Thorough Investigation from the French Authorities. Madam Yi, the wife of Section Chief Yi Renzhi of the First Branch of the First District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, took a girl with her in a private chartered car to visit relatives in the French Concession at around 9 p.m. on the 23rd of last month. While passing the Taohuagong Restaurant at the southern end of the Great World on Avenue Edward VII, a large man in a short silk shirt and pants stopped the chartered car and ordered Madam Yi to get out of the car and accompany him. Madam Yi, seeing that the man looked fierce and suspecting that he was up to no good, refused sternly. Passersby stopped to watch, blocking the road. While they were in a dilemma, Lu Ying, the captain of the Public Security Bureau's Detective Team, was at a banquet at the YMCA. Lu's guard, Mr. Hong, noticed the crowd and, fearing an accident, pushed his way through the crowd. He saw Madam Yi, the wife of Section Chief Yi, and her daughter in the chartered car. Hong was familiar with Madam Yi, so he questioned the large man. The large man said that Hong was meddling in his business and claimed to be surnamed Yang, a detective from the French Concession's gambling squad. He said that he was patrolling and saw Madam Yi in fancy clothes and makeup and suspected that she was a prostitute, so he wanted to arrest her. Hong asked if he had a detective license. Yang replied that he did not have his license with him, and he took out a handgun and handcuffs to prove his identity. Hong also showed his handgun for self-defense. Yang then realized his mistake and left angrily. Section Chief Yi was extremely angry when he heard about the incident. He thought that since the detective was a public official of the police department, he should have undergone some training and have the appropriate judgment and knowledge to perform his duties. Now, the detective was not carrying a license while on duty and was only carrying a handgun. He could not distinguish between good and bad and stopped the car on the road. If someone suspected him of being a highway robber and an accident occurred, who would be responsible? Moreover, Madam Yi is plump, over thirty years old, and with a girl. It is obvious that she is a respectable woman. Now, the detective did not even have this basic knowledge. In the future, whenever a respectable woman passes through the French Concession in fancy clothes and makeup, everyone will feel insecure and have no protection. Therefore, Section Chief Yi translated a formal letter into French a few days ago (last Saturday) and sent it directly to the French Concession police authorities, requesting a thorough investigation and attention to this matter.

The Fierce Competition in the Petroleum Industry Will Tend Towards Compromise and Equal Sales 209

The Price of Kerosene May Rise Slightly

The three major companies that control the petroleum industry, namely Mobil, Asiatic Petroleum Company, and Deutsche Vacuum Oel AG, have branch companies and agencies throughout the country since they started selling in China. However, recently, Russian oil has been dumped in China, and the Guanghua Oil Company, managed by Chinese, has been appointed as the agent, thus starting a fierce competition. Currently, the price of gasoline in this port is uniformly marked at 8 cents per gallon by Mobil and the other three major companies, but the net price is only 6.8 cents when purchased wholesale from Guanghua, while Mobil and the other three companies sell it at 7 cents. Guanghua is 2 cents cheaper than other companies. Yesterday, a reporter from the Guowen News Agency visited Guanghua specifically. According to the director of its gasoline department, the company's sales performance in the first six months of the 22nd year of the Republic of China (1933) was 1.4 million gallons of gasoline and 1.5 million boxes of kerosene (10 gallons per box). The source is entirely from the Russian Oil Export Company, with production originating in Batum, Russia. Recently, the company has divided the country into four central regions: first, Shanghai, which includes the surrounding provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang; second, Hong Kong; third, Hankou; and fourth, Qingdao. The reason why the North China center is located in Qingdao instead of Tianjin or Beijing is because the North China kerosene business is currently contracted to the Dahua Company. The company now prices its products the same as other companies. In reality, other companies cannot further reduce prices to compete. Therefore, in the near future, gasoline prices are unlikely to fluctuate drastically, while kerosene prices may rise slightly. The reporter asked if Guanghua had signed an agreement with other companies to equalize sales and stop lowering prices in order to reach a compromise. The response was that there was no written agreement, but there had been considerable verbal negotiation. Therefore, they will seek a compromise through understanding and temporarily stop competing to avoid further losses.

The Completion and Opening of the Hongkou Isolation Hospital 210

The Isolation Hospital at the intersection of Hujiamu Bridge and Yucai Road in this port held a ceremony on the afternoon of the 30th (the day before yesterday) at 3 p.m. to commemorate the completion of its building. More than 300 people from all walks of life attended. After the meeting, Director Zhu Jingan first reported the purpose of the meeting and the fundraising process. Representatives from the Municipal Party Department and the Fourth District Party Department, Shen Ding; the Health Bureau, Zhao Jinghui; the Social Affairs Bureau, Fu Gunian; the Shanbei Firefighting Joint Association, Li Yanchun; the Wuhua Tianbao Road Commercial Association, Chen Dingan; and guest speaker lawyer Zhang Ji all gave speeches. They all attributed the success to the enthusiastic cooperation of Director Zhu Jingan, Chen Silan, Shen Huachen, economic directors Wang Shenfu and Zhang Peishen, medical directors Lin Chunshan and Zhu Xiaofang, and administrative directors Tang Jingshou and Dong Gengsan. After refreshments, a group photo was taken on the roof terrace, and then the guests were guided through the hospital building before dispersing.

Seeking Corrections and Criticisms for the Shen Bao Yearbook 211

The Shen Bao Yearbook covers a wide range of topics, including land, population, politics, economics, national defense, education, and more than twenty other major categories, encompassing all materials related to Chinese affairs, as well as an outline of world knowledge. It also includes a practical handbook, making it a reference book needed by people from all walks of life. Since its publication, it has been extremely popular in society. The Shen Bao Yearbook Society is deeply concerned that the scope of the book is too broad, and errors are inevitable. It has separately requested review and correction from national political organizations, social groups, and specialized scholars in order to make corrections. The Society has now received more than 200 replies from various parties, mostly expressing satisfaction. For example, the Secretariat of the Legislative Yuan replied, "The collection is extensive, the editing is meticulous, and it is truly a monumental work." The Examination Yuan replied, "Overall, it is appropriate and requires no supplementation." The Ministry of Communications replied, "The content is rich, the tables are detailed, it is a monumental compilation, and it is a valuable reference." Other central government agencies, provincial governments and civil affairs departments, and organizations have also responded. Recently, several experts and readers of the Yearbook have directly questioned discrepancies between statistics published in the Yearbook and those found elsewhere. In addition to carefully verifying the basis and replying separately, the Society has also found errors due to careless proofreading in the book. Therefore, it is specifically re-checking and preparing to print an errata sheet to distribute to readers, as well as conducting its own review under more than 1,500 detailed items. However, omissions may still be inevitable. Therefore, this advertisement is published to solicit criticism from experts and readers, and to inform them of any errors they find.

Publishing World 212

The sales of "The Female Voice" semi-monthly magazine, published by The Female Voice Society, have increased sharply during the summer vacation. This is largely because the contributors to the magazine are all leading women from various fields. In the literary world, there are Su Mei, Lu Yin, Wu Shutian, and others. From the legal world, there is Zhou Shu, Chen Lingyi, and others. They are all long-term contributors to the magazine. Therefore, the articles are short, concise, stimulating, and powerful, keeping readers engaged. Compared to other women's magazines, it can be said to be unique. It is reported that Volume 1, Issue 21 will be published today. Important articles include "Hard Work, Quick Work, Solid Work," "Sour but Still Acceptable," "The Relief of Modern Young Women's Troubles," "The Good Fortune of a Wang Family Young Madam," "Photographs of Couple's Life," "In Memory of Ms. Ding Ling," "After Losing Love," etc. The magazine is priced low, with 24 issues per year. The subscription price for other cities is 1.2 yuan per year, and for this city it is 1 yuan. It is also reported that various bookstores and newsstands sell the magazine.

The International Daily Anthology, published by China Publishing Company, follows "Scientific Knowledge" and is co-edited by Sun Shiyi, Ming Yaowu, and others. The International Daily Anthology recruits more than 100 translators to provide translations and was published today. Its special issue is themed "Fifteen Years of the Soviet Union's Foreign Trade Monopoly." It is truly a comprehensive review of international periodicals and a great compilation of encyclopedic commentary. The price is low, with a pre-ordered price of 1.2 yuan for two months, not including postage, and a retail price of 4 cents. Ordinary issues are only sold for 2 cents.

Its sanitary equipment includes bathtubs as usual, and a large public bath is specially opened for guests to enjoy. It is especially suitable for both elegant and popular tastes. As for water heating, elevators, gardens, lounges, Chinese and Western food, everything is available and strives for perfection. The waiters and servants are selected from famous hotels and given new training, so the service is incomparable to the old style. It is now being decorated and will be opened on an auspicious day as soon as it is completed, which will surely add a unique color to Shanghai. It is also heard that the hotel has newly written a book called "Notes on Tourism Service," which is compiled based on decades of experience. It is also sold by the hotel's preparatory office (inside Hongyu Lane on Zhengjia Muqiao). The content is rich and is a must-read for those engaged in the tourism industry. Medicine 215

Changzhou Native Place Association Provides Medical Care The Changzhou Native Place Association has provided free medical consultations and medicine every summer, but it has been limited to the central district, which is not widespread enough. This year, it has created a special method of entrusting medical consultations and providing medicine nearby. The method has been enthusiastically taken up by famous doctors Ding Zhongying, Ji Hongyuan, Zhu Shaowu, Zhu Baoliang, Wang Ansheng, Guo Zhongliang, Sheng Xinru, Chen Yaotang, Chen Daoming, Zhang Boxi, Zhang Zanchen, Zhang Zuhua, Zhang Xuchu, Zhang Lan'an, Fei Zibin, Xie Liheng, Jiang Maoyuan, Wang Tinghua. The association has printed consultation coupons and distributed them to various committee members, team leaders, doctors, and pharmacies for nearby distribution. It has also printed two-part medicine coupons and distributed them to doctors for use. Agreements have also been reached with major pharmacies in various districts to dispense medicine upon presentation of the coupons. From now on, poor and sick fellow villagers from Changzhou can enjoy practical benefits.

The 33rd District Citizen's Association Provides Medical Care The 33rd District Branch of the Shanghai First Special District Citizen's Association, in view of the narrow living conditions of Shanghai citizens and the recent heat wave, when the climate is unstable, has found that even a slight oversight can lead to serious illness. The association has been limited by finances and procrastination, often leading to loss of life. It has been approved at the fifth regular meeting to hire Western medicine doctor Fei Boqing and traditional Chinese medicine doctor Yang Huanzhang as voluntary summer doctors for the association, to provide consultations and medicine. The time for Western medicine consultations is from 4:30 p.m. to 5:30 p.m. every day, and the time for traditional Chinese medicine consultations is from 6:00 p.m. to 7:00 p.m., with consultations stopping on Sundays. The association's address is No. 4 Xilian Lane, at the intersection of Guangxi Road and Shantou Road. The service starts today.

The Establishment of the People's Health Advisory Society The People's Health Advisory Society, founded by traditional Chinese medicine doctor Gu Yushi, aims to treat and cure diseases and guide health for the people with a spirit of sacrifice. The society has announced its establishment, and people from Nanshi, Zhabei, and the concessions have enthusiastically joined the society. In order to facilitate the public's membership, there are more than 20 specially appointed contact points in the three districts. Detailed information can be obtained by sending a letter with postage to the general office at No. 11 Yingsheng Lane, Haishan Road, Wusong.

Letter to the Editor 217

To the Editor: The news item published in today's edition of your newspaper, under the "Local News" column, regarding the relocation of the Marine Products and Sundries Association back to its original address, is inaccurate. The building at Dianchun Hall, located at the City God Temple, is owned by our association. On the 29th of this month, a group claiming to be members of the Marine Products Industry Association forcibly entered the premises. Our association is currently seeking legal remedies. The original article contained inaccuracies. We respectfully request that you publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" column to correct the record. Sincerely, Shanghai Sugar Industry Association. July 31.

To the Editor: On July 21st, your newspaper published a news item about a fire at Yao Xingchang Machinery Factory on Xiaoshadu Road. In fact, the fire occurred at a business next door to Yao Xingchang, and thankfully, the fire trucks arrived quickly and extinguished the fire. Yao Xingchang suffered no losses whatsoever. We are deeply concerned that the outside world may misunderstand and that our business will be affected. Therefore, we are writing to your newspaper to request that you publish a correction in the "Letters to the Editor" column. Sincerely, Yao Xingchang. July 31.

Over the Yangtze River basin and the coastal areas including this city, cloudy and hot, with winds from the southeast to northeast, and occasional local showers. Education News

Important News: Jiangxi Province's Junior and Senior High School Entrance Examinations Proceed Smoothly 220

Elementary School Results Better than High School; Schools Outside the Provincial Capital Worse than those in the Capital. Cheng Shih-kuei, Director of the Jiangxi Provincial Department of Education, was ordered to handle the graduation examinations for elementary and secondary schools. Due to thorough preparation and strict security measures, the process has been proceeding smoothly. The province's high schools were divided into six districts, and five provincial supervisors, Xiao Qian, Ouyang Kui, Zhou Ke-gang, Tu Lin, and Long Cheng, were appointed to head the examination offices at each district's testing location. Principals of various secondary schools and magistrates of the counties where the districts were located were also appointed as supervising commissioners to assist in the process. However, due to inconvenient transportation in the fourth district, Yichun and Pingxiang were divided into two testing locations. Provincial Supervisor Shao De-ji was specially dispatched to Pingxiang to oversee the proceedings. The entire province uniformly conducted the examinations on the 26th of last month. The first district, Nanchang, was divided into four testing venues. The first venue, located at the Women's Vocational School, was for the high school students from various schools. The second, third, and fourth venues were located at the Second Middle School, the First Women's Middle School, and the Second Vocational School, and the Third Vocational School respectively, serving as testing locations for junior high school students. Representatives from the provincial government and the court were also invited to supervise the venues. The junior high school examinations lasted three consecutive days, and the high school examinations lasted four consecutive days. Over 800 junior high school students and over 140 high school students in the first district were able to submit their papers on time. Reports from other districts have also been successively sent back to the province. The elementary school graduation examinations were held on the 29th and 30th. A total of 650 students from 36 elementary schools in Nanchang participated in the examinations. Four students, who were temporarily ill, did not take the exam. Officials at the Department of Education have been extremely busy reviewing the examination results submitted by various elementary and secondary schools, and this process is nearing completion. It is said that elementary school results are better than those of high schools, while the results of high schools outside the provincial capital are worse than those in the capital. Although the results are not entirely satisfactory, the overall order of the provincial examinations was satisfactory, and no other incidents occurred. This is considered passable.

The Ministry of Education Recently Announced Four Curriculum Standards (Part 2) 221

(2) Junior High School Drawing

First Goal

(1) To stimulate students' aesthetic instincts, cultivate their temperament, and enable students to understand the relationship between art and life, in order to enhance the meaning of their lives. (2) To enable students to practice their observation skills and descriptive skills regarding human figures and natural forms. (3) To instill in students artistic truths, common knowledge, and skills, in order to cultivate their ability to use art to cope with the environment.

Second Time Allocation

Two hours per week in the first and second academic years, and one hour per week in the third academic year.

Third Curriculum Outline

(1) First Academic Year

(1) Form depiction exercises, position, composition basics, etc. (2) The relationship between light and dark, and distance, in form. (3) The differences in light and dark in indoor and outdoor light. (4) The relationship between light and dark, distance, and color. Color harmony and its matching methods. (5) Parallel perspective drawing. (6) Natural beauty depiction exercises. (7) A brief introduction to the origin of art.

(2) Second Academic Year

(1) Still life and landscape depiction exercises. (2) Free expression exercises of color, form composition, and thoughts. (3) Angular perspective drawing. (4) The true meaning of art, and a brief introduction to the characteristics and evolution of Chinese and Western art. (5) Pattern drawing.

(3) Third Academic Year

(1) Geometric drawing. (2) Sketching or pattern composition. (3) Work design drawing. Note: The above three items should be emphasized according to the school's environment and needs.

Fourth Implementation Method Summary 222

(1) Assignment Requirements

(1) Observation and appreciation. 1. Illustrations. 2. Methods of observing real objects. 3. Research on natural appreciation. 4. Guidance on appreciating famous works. (2) Practice. 1. Sketching. 2. Memory depiction training. 3. Assigned topic exercises. 4. Free creation. 5. Pattern composition method. 6. Diagram production.

(2) Teaching Method Key Points

(1) Relying on Chinese and Western painting methods and materials, students practice preliminary methods such as observation and depiction, and use theoretical methods at any time to guide students to develop sound thoughts and skills. 1. The materials should be novel, in line with students' interests, and beneficial to their physical and mental health. 2. The reasoning should be simple and clear, and in line with students' level and age. 3. The guidance and correction of skills must be practical and legitimate, but not too detailed. (2) At any time, stimulate students' interest in artworks and the natural world, and develop the habit of automatic research and production. 1. Joint research when decorating school venues and classrooms. 2. Visit various art groups and participate in work. 3. Design and guidance on matters related to students' personal affairs. 4. Teachers must be diligent in research and set an example. 5. It is advisable to use field trips or travel sketching to increase the interest in practice. (3) The results of practice and appreciation should gradually influence the body and mind, so as to become the foundation of perfect character. 1. Famous works and art news should be explained and announced frequently to broaden students' knowledge. 2. There should be facilities for various levels of competition and exhibitions within the school. 3. Select painter biographies and other materials related to students' thoughts and skills, and give limited-time lectures to promote students' self-awareness. 4. Guide students to practice criticism to enhance their discrimination ability. 5. Award or announce students' excellent works to promote the efforts of all students. 6. Slogan, news painting and other exercises guidance. (4) For the environment, one should develop a sensitivity to beauty and ugliness. 1. Students should participate in the reform design of a certain part of the school, and practice thinking and drawing. 2. Collect uncommon things at any time, and let students distinguish their beauty and ugliness. For the same things, students should also be allowed to explain their individual characteristics. 3. Let students practice mutual evaluation of their exercises. (5) There should be considerable contact with other courses. 1. Composition exercises on historical materials, stories, ideal paintings, etc. 2. Satirical exercises on world events and Chinese current affairs. 3. Design and construction exercises on industrial, commercial, agricultural, and architectural operations. 4. Simple depiction exercises on natural life forms. 5. Expression exercises of free thoughts.

(3) Senior High School Drawing 223

First Goal

(1) To continue to cultivate the virtues and interests of beauty. (2) To increase the production capacity of applied art. (3) To improve the level of drawing, as a preparation for further study. (4) To cultivate the creative ability to express thoughts and feelings, in order to promote the realization of a new life.

Second Time Allocation 224

One hour per week in the first academic year, two hours per week in the second academic year, and two hours per week in the third academic year.

Third Curriculum Outline 225

(1) First Academic Year

(1) For basic drawing methods such as plaster statues, still lifes, and landscapes, continue the study of junior high school, and make accurate and appropriate depiction exercises. (2) Research on various drawing methods of pencil drawing, charcoal drawing, and watercolor painting. (3) Pattern composition method. (4) An overview of art and a superficial discussion of image aesthetics.

(2) Second Academic Year

(1) Composition method of complex subjects. (2) Pattern composition method. (3) Projection drawing. (4) Work design drawing.

(3) Third Academic Year

(1) Projection drawing. (2) Pattern making. (3) Preliminary mechanical drawing. (4) An overview of arts and crafts. Note: In addition to lecturing on the outline of arts and crafts, the above four items should be emphasized according to the school's environment and needs.

Fourth Implementation Method Summary 226

1. Assignment Requirements

(1) Research and Appreciation. (1) Comparative view of the content and methods of Chinese and Western painting, architecture, and sculpture. (2) The principles of art, craft, and social evolution. (3) Comparative view of the spirit of ancient, modern and other famous works. (2) Practice. (1) Practice common skills and production in art. (2) Practice pattern making. (A) Pattern organization method. (B) Biological image change method. (C) Design pattern. (3) (Research on the principles of drawing and practice on the beauty of technology.

(2) Teaching Method Key Points

(1) The selection of research teaching materials should be based on those that are suitable for the level of ordinary high school and can develop their knowledge and feelings equally. (2) The selection of practical teaching materials should be based on the current cultivation of students and beneficial to future further education, or general applications. (3) In terms of assignment, we must always pay attention to correcting their radical ideas and bad technical styles. (4) In terms of appreciation, do not let students flow into negative, decadent and other tendencies that are not conducive to young people. (5) In terms of creation, we must follow their free interests and express them smoothly. It is not advisable to be harsh on comments, and it is especially not advisable to use special methods or factions to prevent the development of their talents. (6) Teachers must be in a guiding position and use moral sentiment to influence young people.

Important Telegram on the Resolution of the Anhui Education Uprising 227

The Provincial Department of Education wired the resolution process: Since the outbreak of this provincial capital education uprising, all parties have attached great importance to it. The newspapers have reported it. Chairman Liu has repeatedly telegraphed the Department of Education from Guangxi to inquire about it and instructed on the handling policy. After investigation, the incident has been handled calmly by the Provincial Government and the Department of Education. The Central Government and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek have dealt with it severely, and it has now been completely quelled. It is reported that the Anhui Provincial Department of Education yesterday reported the handling process to Chairman Liu by telegram. The original telegrams of Chairman Liu and the Department of Education are extracted as follows:

Chairman Liu's Respectful Telegram to the Department of Education: "To Governor Ma and Director Yang of the Provincial Government, I have received the telegrams and attachments from Brothers Lingfu and Haodian, and Brother Simo and Xiaodian. They are stored in secret. Because the communists are rampant and I am engaged in the suppression, I have no time to take care of Anhui's political affairs, so I have repeatedly telegraphed, advocating a peaceful settlement. Recently, I received a telegram from Brother Simo and Xiaodian, and learned about the entire process. The accommodation and compromise have been meticulous, and the sabotage of a few individuals is a disgrace to the education community of Anhui. Brother Lingfu's telegram reported that Xie Jiaxi and other faculty and staff of the high school actually destroyed the Director's office and injured the staff. Such out-of-bounds actions are obviously a violation of criminal law and should be handed over to the court for legal action. Fortunately, the examinations have been completed and do not affect the students. The two high schools, No. 1 Middle School, can be reorganized calmly. The future of education is cause for celebration. This is a special reply. Respectfully, Liu Zhenhua."

The Department of Education's Grateful Telegram to Chairman Liu: "To Chairman Liu in Guangxi, I have received your secret telegram, and I am very grateful for everything. Since I took office, I have followed your instructions to be pragmatic and realistic in Anhui's education, and strive for rectification. At the beginning of taking office, I immediately handled the examination matters. All measures were carefully considered according to laws and facts, and strived to be implemented without obstruction. Although I relied on your virtue and power to enable the vast majority of students to take the exam willingly, due to my lack of virtue and prestige, the disturbances were inevitable. I have served without any similarity and have not had time to wait for punishment. I am very grateful for your praise in the telegram. After reading it, I only increase my shame and fear. After that, I should work harder to live up to your expectations. Now the examination matters have been completely concluded, and the aftermath of the disturbance has also been handled carefully in accordance with acting Chairman Ma. The principals who failed to handle the examinations have been dismissed by the Provincial Government meeting. The new principals are also taking over in order. Xie Hongsheng and other faculty and staff who disrupted the office have been ordered by the Provincial Government to be arrested. Li Guansan has been arrested and handed over to the court for legal judgment. Now the new academic year is about to begin. Because I have received telegrams from Chairman Chiang of the Executive Yuan's Ministry of Education and your order to rectify education in a timely manner to eliminate accumulated malpractices, I have reported to the Provincial Government and made appropriate changes to the principals of provincial schools, in order to make people worthy of their posts. In the future, all reforms are being planned comprehensively, and I will report to acting Chairman Ma for handling at any time, and ask you to give instructions when you are free from military affairs, so that I can follow and avoid being negligent. The original telegram of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek was sent to you. The original text is: "To Chairman Liu Xueya of Anqing, the educational elements in Anhui Province are complicated and the content is not good. The situation below middle schools is even worse. Now it is the summer vacation. I hope you will instruct Director Yang of the Education Department to seriously rectify and strive to improve, which is very fortunate. Zhongzheng Yuanji Gu Yin." It should be reported to you by acting Chairman Ma. The details may have been reported to you by acting Chairman Ma. Combine the statements, Minister of Education Yang Lian respectfully."

Local News

Remainder of the Municipal Education Association's Donation for the Righteous Army Allocated to the Aviation Association to Purchase "Shanghai School" Aircraft 228

The total amount is more than 16,000 yuan. The naming ceremony is scheduled for the 12th. The Municipal Education Association once made a donation for the anti-Japanese righteous army. The amount of the donation was a total of 18,145 yuan and 8 jiao. In addition to being announced in the newspapers, a letter of appreciation has been printed and distributed to each donor. In addition to the payments made to the Rehe Anti-Japanese Army and the慰勞 (wèi láo) consolation fees for the anti-Japanese soldiers in Northeast China, there is a remaining balance of 16,085 yuan and 2 jiao. The original plan was to continue to remit the remaining balance to the anti-Japanese righteous army, but the righteous army retreated and could not be remitted. Later, it was proposed to remit it to Moscow for the consulate to forward it, but there was no reply from the consulate. The Education Association immediately convened a meeting of principals of all schools and donors. At the meeting, it was decided that since there was no proper way to remit the remaining balance, it would be appropriate to use it to purchase the "Shanghai School" aircraft. The "Shanghai School" aircraft has now been ordered from the Aviation Association and arrived in Shanghai, and the naming ceremony can be held on August 12. The remaining balance has also been informed by the Municipal Education Association to the Aviation Association for collection, and it will be used to purchase the "Shanghai School" aircraft.

"Shanghai Boy Scouts" Aircraft to be Named 229

It has been decided to be on the 10th of this month, at Jiangwan or Hongqiao. The Shanghai Council of the Boy Scouts of China previously organized a recruitment committee to raise funds for the Boy Scouts aircraft, and elected Tong Xingbai as the chief captain, and the captains of each group as captains. Because it is related to saving the country, all Boy Scouts in the city worked very hard, and as a result, more than 20,000 yuan was raised. It is now reported that after the second batch of aircraft from the Shanghai Aviation Association arrived in Shanghai, the Boy Scouts Council yesterday specially wrote to the Aviation Association, designating one aircraft in the batch as the "Shanghai Boy Scouts" aircraft, and the naming ceremony will be held on the 10th of this month at the same time. The number of members of the presidium was also determined. The Situation of the Competition between Wang and Sun 235

Wang won again with 6 to 3. His backhand is slightly weaker, and his online play has no special features. His serve is sure and has little hard work. However, if Yu Tianguang can go online and get the right method, he may be able to win Wang. If he uses baseline shots, Wang can definitely win. In any case, there will be a fierce battle between Yu and Wang today.

In this year's competition, if Ke Xian defeated Pan Lai on the first day, he could continue to maintain his victory. Ke Xian Defeated Austin 238

Each won two sets. In the first group of the competition, in the first three sets, the score was 5-7, 6-4, 4-6. Austin took the lead, and the situation was unfavorable for Ke Xian. Ke Xian tried his best to cheer up and managed to tie the score to 3 to 3. Austin forced Ke Xian to stay at the baseline with a deep forehand, so he was able to take the lead with 4 to 3. Ke Xian then made it 4 to 4 and took the lead with 5 to 4, and finally

won with 6 to 4.

In the final battle, at the beginning of the last set, both sides won one game each. Austin took the lead with 2 to 1, followed by 3 to 1 and 4 to 2. Austin's victory seemed to be beyond doubt. However, Ke Xian made every effort to attack and made Austin run around the field, not having time to return the attack. Austin wanted to intercept online, but Ke Xian stopped him with a high ball. Pan Lei Defeats Mo Lin 239

However, Mo Lin did not lose hope, returning every ball sent his way, earning applause from the audience for his brilliant plays. However, Pan Lei launched a fierce counterattack, using powerful forehand shots to tie the score at three to three, followed by four to three. Mo Lin then won two consecutive games, taking the lead again at five to four, and had two opportunities to win the set, but unfortunately missed both. Pan also had three opportunities to win, but Mo Lin managed to win back one game, tying the score at six to six. Despite his best efforts, Pan Lei proved to be the superior player. Mo Lin won the first game, but Pan Lei then won four consecutive games, taking the lead at four to one. Mo won back one game, making it four to two, but Pan Lei eventually won the third set six to two.

After each side won one game, Pan Lei used long-distance forehand shots to hit the corners of the court, forcing Mo Lin to run around and make difficult returns, giving Pan a four to one lead. At this point, Mo Lin returned a ball, but the landing point was not very clear, and Pan Lei was unable to return it, showing signs of frustration. Mo Lin seized the opportunity to tie the score at four to four, then five to five, but his strength was exhausted at this point. Pan gradually won two consecutive games, ultimately winning with a score of seven to five.

National Games Organizing Committee to Take Over Site This Morning 241

Chief Director Chu, Deputy Chief Director Zhang Xinfu, Deputy Chief Director Wu Yunrui, and members of the organizing committee Hao Gengsheng, Yuan Dunli, Shen Siliang, Ma Xun, Zhang Jiong, Xu Yusheng, Du Tingxiu, and heads of various departments including Lei Zhen (General Affairs), Wu Zhuozhi (Transportation), Xu Yanzi (Prizes), and Peng Baichuan (Documentation), totaling more than ten people, traveled to the Central Stadium by Jiangnan Changsui car at 7:30 AM on the 30th to inspect the site. The purpose was to decide on issues such as the installation of water and electricity, as well as how to repair and renovate the facility. Director Zhang led the inspection of the various competition venues and the track. They finished around 10:00 AM and returned to the city. The current condition of the Central Stadium is briefly described below:

(1) The Central Stadium is located at the southern foot of Zhongshan Mountain, in the southeast corner of Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum, about eight li from the city. It can be reached directly by public bus, which takes about 25 minutes. Construction of the stadium began in 1930 and was completed in 1931, costing approximately 1.6 million yuan. After the 1931 National Games were cancelled, the entire facility fell into disuse. Only the swimming pool was open briefly last summer. This year, due to insufficient water supply, it has not reopened. The Mausoleum Management Committee spends 2,000 yuan per month to maintain the facility, and employs a number of staff to manage the site. The minutes of the third working meeting of the stadium on July 25 are supplemented below, which show a general picture of the work + situation: Attendees included Lin Huguang, Hua Guangli, Fu Huangguang, Huang Ziquan, Fei Jizong, and Wang Rulin. Matters decided upon: (1) Regarding gardens, grass laying, and sunflower fertilization, the matter will be submitted to Chairman Lin for handling. The weeds in the entire stadium are too overgrown and should be removed selectively. The garden engineering work for the 22nd National Games will commence on August 1. (2) Regarding engineering, dredging of the drainage ditches around the football field will continue, as well as repairs to the sidewalks on the main road. (3) Regarding general affairs, a general register of furniture for the venue should be created and submitted to the Mausoleum Committee to discuss how to lend it to the 22nd National Games.

(2) The venue is oval-shaped, with concrete stands all around. There is no damage, and it can accommodate approximately 30,000 to 50,000 spectators. The grass on the track in the middle is overgrown, which will be removed urgently, and the track will be re-laid. Both ends of the track are surrounded by wire mesh, which will serve as the finals venues for volleyball, basketball, and national martial arts.

(3) The athletes' dormitories are located under the east and west stands. Each room can accommodate 24 people, and the beds are fully equipped. Running water, bathtubs, and flush toilets are all readily available.

(4) The basketball court is very close to the venue, located northwest of the stadium entrance. It is an open-air court in a sunken style. The concrete stands around it are still in good condition, but the floor is damaged. The National Games Organizing Committee will re-surface and paint it. The martial arts court is located south of the basketball court and has a similar style, but it is circular. The court is made of dirt, and the grass is several feet deep. Measures must be taken to clean it up. There are a total of twelve tennis courts. Except for the court used by the stadium staff, which is still in good condition, the rest all need to be resurfaced. North of the basketball court is the swimming pool. Although the pool is not damaged, there is no water supply. It is reported that the National Games Organizing Committee plans to build a large artesian well to fully supply water to the venue. This project will cost more than 10,000 yuan and must begin construction within days. Opposite the swimming pool is the baseball field. The field is small and may not be suitable for use. In addition, the race track and football field are currently planted with soybeans, which are growing vigorously. It would be a pity to cut them down before they are ripe. It is said that they will be repaired after the harvest.

(5) 136 silver prizes were received for the 20th National Games, and a clear register has been created. Director Xu Yanzi of the Prizes Department has inspected them once, and they will be officially inventoried and transferred for use as prizes for this year's event on August 1. The remaining medals and badges for the organizing committee staff, etc., will all be those already made in 1931, in order to reuse waste and save expenses.

Discussion of Water Supply and Other Issues 242

After the inspection, the standing committee members held a standing committee meeting in the Ministry of Education. The heads of each group also participated in the discussion on the water supply for the venue. It is estimated that the total number of athletes and organizing committee staff during the Games will be no less than 2,000 people. Each person needs at least 50 gallons of water per day (including [drinking] [use]), so the daily water demand must be around 100,000 gallons. In addition, there is also a lack of water source for the swimming pool. Although there are five artesian wells at the venue, only two are usable, which is far from the required amount. As a result of the discussion, it was decided to immediately send a letter to the Ministry of Interior's Health Department requesting them to send personnel to test the well water at the venue. If it is drinkable, the artesian wells will be dredged one by one for drinking. At the same time, a letter will be sent to the municipal government to rush the connection of tap water pipes. However, the estimated cost is over 10,000 yuan, and efforts will be made to save money. Regarding the swimming pool, it is planned to borrow the newly built swimming pool of the Central Military Academy.

Site to be Taken Over Today 243

Regarding the takeover of the site, the organizing committee has agreed with the Mausoleum Management Committee to borrow it for three months starting from August 1, and has appointed Zhang Xinfu, Lei Zhen, and Peng Baichuan to handle the takeover matters. Zhang and others are scheduled to officially take over today. It is said that the first step after the takeover is to handle the water connection and cut the weeds, and delineate the area. The organizing committee's office has decided to temporarily set up two locations. One is the old site of the Ministry of Education's Compilation and Translation Bureau, because the bureau is located within the Ministry of Education. In order to facilitate communication and coordination before the Games, it is planned to borrow the location to handle documentation matters. The other location is the Central Stadium, where the person in charge will handle the site arrangement. They will rush to start working there tomorrow. On September 1, the secretariat will be officially established at the venue.

(Nanjing, July 31) The National Games Organizing Committee held a standing committee meeting on the evening of the 31st to discuss the post-takeover arrangements and issues such as sports rules and funding. The site takeover is scheduled for the morning of the 1st, with Zhang Xinfu and two others going.

Games Budget Must Be Increased 244

The provisional budget for the National Games was originally set at 93,000 yuan by the organizing committee. When it was submitted to the central government for review, it was reduced to 50,000 yuan in view of the current difficult financial situation of the national treasury, and the need to host everything economically. Yesterday, according to Chu Minyi, the organizing committee has only received 5,000 yuan from the Ministry of Finance so far. The organizing committee has budgeted the entire cost at 50,000 yuan, which is definitely not

enough. Furthermore, the site takeover is imminent, and funds are urgently needed. He has telegraphed Chairman Chiang, President Wang, and Minister Zhu, requesting them to find ways to increase the amount to the previous figure, so as to avoid running out of funds when the event arrives.

Hao Gengsheng Talks About the Success of the North China Games 245

The Shanghai Newspaper Association hosted a banquet last night for Hao Gengsheng, Chief Director of the recently concluded North China Games. He recently traveled from Qingdao to Beijing on official business, and arrived in Shanghai from Beijing yesterday. He will return to Qingdao today. The Shanghai Newspaper Association, in recognition of the exceptional cooperation between the North China Games and Shanghai newspapers, especially the contributions of Mr. Hao, specially hosted a banquet at Yizhixiang to welcome him and express gratitude. Sports reporters from various newspapers accompanied him. During the banquet, Mr. Hao reported on the efforts made in organizing the North China Games and some of its successes. His words were sincere and thought-provoking. A brief summary is as follows:

Three years ago in Shenyang, the North China Games were held this time in Qingdao. At that time, given the critical situation in North China, it was like Shenyang three years ago. Although the North China Games had fourteen units, the four northeastern provinces had already fallen into the hands of the Japanese. However, in this difficult situation, colleagues were even more determined to strive for success. They were cautious and worked together in a spirit of cooperation. The success of the North China Games this time was due to the full cooperation of all parties. The spirit of cooperation can be recorded as one.

The result of "foolish" hard work. Many people expressed doubts about holding the North China Games in Qingdao. Especially since Qingdao does not have many schools and is a mixed community of Chinese and foreigners, improper measures could damage the entire North China sports. In terms of venues, after some painstaking negotiations, they were obtained from foreigners. Therefore, all measures were taken carefully and carried out according to plan to avoid giving people excuses. The opening ceremony, awarding of prizes, and all ceremonies were modeled after the Olympic Games. From the opening to the closing, everything was orderly, leaving a good impression. Therefore, after the closing ceremony, a Western newspaper in Qingdao, which had previously launched attacks, wrote a long and favorable review, praising it extensively. The conclusion only said that what was lacking was weak performance. The success of the North China Games is said by some to be the result of our "foolish" hard work.

A glimpse of the results. The results achieved by the North China Games this time are incomparable to the Far East and the world. Foreigners will laugh when they hear it, and Chinese people will laugh when they see it. However, as a result of hard work, eight national records were broken, twelve North China records were broken, two equaled national records, and thirty-five individuals broke records. This is still somewhat comforting in the midst of disappointment. Shanghai's sports have more opportunities to come into contact with foreigners, so progress is easier than in North China. We deeply hope that we will all promote it and work together to raise our country's records day by day.
